--!native
local collectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local triangleFill = require(script.TriangleFill)
local convexHull = require(script.ConvexHull)

local module = {}

module.planes = {}
module.colors = {}

module.debugTris = {}

module.depthBuffer = {}
module.debugDepthBuffer = {}
module.debugPixels = {}
module.xCount = 0
module.yCount = 0
module.dynamicVisRecords = {}
module.occluderRecords = {}
module.stats = {}
 
module.debugGui = nil
module.occlusionTime = {}
module.occlusionTimeAvg = 0
module.checkDynamicVisTime = {}
module.checkDynamicVisTimeAvg = 0


--Settings
module.allowDebug = script.Parent:GetAttribute("allowDebugInLive") or (game.ReplicatedFirst:FindFirstChild("allowDebugInLive")~=nil)
--Always allow it in studio
if (game["Run Service"]:IsStudio() == true) then
	module.allowDebug = true
end

module.debugging = false and module.allowDebug
module.drawDebugText = script.parent:GetAttribute("enableDebugOnStart") and module.allowDebug

module.override = false
module.debugging = false
module.debugTextPos =0

local numPixelsTested = 0

local corners = {
	Vector3.new(-0.5,-0.5,-0.5),
	Vector3.new( 0.5,-0.5,-0.5),
	Vector3.new(-0.5, 0.5,-0.5),
	Vector3.new( 0.5, 0.5,-0.5),
	Vector3.new(-0.5,-0.5, 0.5),
	Vector3.new( 0.5,-0.5, 0.5),
	Vector3.new(-0.5, 0.5, 0.5),
	Vector3.new( 0.5, 0.5, 0.5)
}

local function PlaneFromPoints(v0,v1,v2)
	local xx = v1 - v0
	local yy = v2 - v0
	local normal = xx:Cross(yy)
	normal = normal.Unit
	
	local res = {
		n = normal,
		d = -v0:Dot(normal)
	}
	
	return res
end

function module:InitColors()
	if (self.colorsInited ~= true) then
		self.colorsInited = true
		self.colors = {}
		for j=1,1000 do
			table.insert(self.colors , Color3.fromHSV(math.random(),0.5, 0.5))
		end

		self.dynamicVisRecords.__mode = "k"
		self.occluderRecords.__mode = "k"
	end
end
 
 
function module:BuildWOrldToViewportCFrame(camera)

	local viewportSize = camera.ViewportSize
	local aspectRatio = viewportSize.X / viewportSize.Y
	local fov = math.rad(camera.FieldOfView)
	local nearPlane = 0.1 -- Near clipping plane
	local farPlane = 1000 -- Far clipping plane

	-- Projection matrix (perspective)
	
	CFrame.new()
	
	local projectionMatrix = Matrix.new(
		1 / (aspectRatio * math.tan(fov / 2)), 0, 0, 0,
		0, 1 / math.tan(fov / 2), 0, 0,
		0, 0, farPlane / (farPlane - nearPlane), 1,
		0, 0, (-farPlane * nearPlane) / (farPlane - nearPlane), 0
	)

	-- View matrix (camera's inverse transformation)
	local cameraCFrame = camera.CFrame
	local viewMatrix = cameraCFrame:Inverse()

	-- World to viewport matrix
	return projectionMatrix * viewMatrix
	

end
 
function module:Update()
	
	local camera = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera
	
	self:PreDrawDebug()
	 
	self:BuildFrustumPlanes(camera)
	self:RenderOccluders(camera)
	self:DrawDebug()
end

function module:PreDrawDebug()
	debug.profilebegin("PreDrawDebug")
	
	if (self.debugGui == nil) then
		self.debugGui = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("DebugPixels", true)
		self.debugBox = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("DebugPixelBox", true)
	end

	for key,tri in self.debugTris do
		tri:Destroy()
	end
	self.debugTris = {}

	for key,pixel in self.debugPixels do
		pixel:Destroy()		
	end
	self.debugPixels = {}
	debug.profileend()
end

function module:DrawDebug()
	if (self.debugging == true) then
		debug.profilebegin("DrawDebug")
		
		self:DrawOccludedBoundingBox()
		
		local x = self.xCount
		for key,value in self.depthBuffer do

			local y = math.floor(key / x)
			local x = key - (y * x)

			self:RenderDebugPixel(x,y, value)
		end
		
		--[[
		local x = self.xCount
		for key,value in self.debugDepthBuffer do

			local y = math.floor(key / x)
			local x = key - (y * x)

			self:RenderDebugPixelRed(x,y, value)
		end]]--

		debug.profileend()
	end	
	
	if (self.drawDebugText) then
		self:PrintStats()
	end
end

function module:BuildFrustumPlanes(camera )
	debug.profilebegin("BuildFrustums")
	--[[
	
			top view
			            b1
				a1 	
			C
				c1
						d1
	]]--
	
	local x = camera.ViewportSize.X
	local y = camera.ViewportSize.Y
	
	local far = 20000
	local yCount = 20
	self.yPixelSize = math.floor(y / yCount)
	local xCount = math.ceil(x / self.yPixelSize)+1 

	self.xCount = xCount
	self.yCount = yCount
 
	local blockSize = math.ceil(self.yPixelSize / 2)+1
	local a1 = camera:ViewportPointToRay(-blockSize, -blockSize,0)
	local c1 = camera:ViewportPointToRay(x + blockSize*2, -blockSize,0)
	local a2 = camera:ViewportPointToRay(-blockSize, y + blockSize,0)
	local c2 = camera:ViewportPointToRay(x + blockSize*2, y + blockSize,0)
		 		
	local ra1 = a1.Origin + a1.Direction  
	local ra2 = a2.Origin + a2.Direction  
	local rb1 = a1.Origin + a1.Direction * far
	local rb2 = a2.Origin + a2.Direction * far
	local rc1 = c1.Origin + c1.Direction  
	local rc2 = c2.Origin + c2.Direction  
	local rd1 = c1.Origin + c1.Direction * far
	local rd2 = c2.Origin + c2.Direction * far
		
	--build some planes
	self.outerPlanes = {}
	self.outerPlanes[1] = PlaneFromPoints(ra1, rc1, ra2) --near
	--self.outerPlanes = planes[2] = PlaneFromPoints(rb1, rb2,rd1) --far 
	
	self.outerPlanes[2] = PlaneFromPoints(ra1,rb1,rc1) --top
	self.outerPlanes[3] = PlaneFromPoints(ra1,ra2,rb1) --left
	self.outerPlanes[4] = PlaneFromPoints(ra2,rc2,rb2)--bot
	self.outerPlanes[5] = PlaneFromPoints(rc1,rd1,rd2)  --right
 	
	
	--Inner planes
	local a1 = camera:ViewportPointToRay(0, 0, 0)
	local c1 = camera:ViewportPointToRay(x, 0, 0)
	local a2 = camera:ViewportPointToRay(0, y ,0)
	local c2 = camera:ViewportPointToRay(x, y ,0)
	
	local ra1 = a1.Origin + a1.Direction  
	local ra2 = a2.Origin + a2.Direction  
	local rb1 = a1.Origin + a1.Direction * far
	local rb2 = a2.Origin + a2.Direction * far
	local rc1 = c1.Origin + c1.Direction  
	local rc2 = c2.Origin + c2.Direction  
	local rd1 = c1.Origin + c1.Direction * far
	local rd2 = c2.Origin + c2.Direction * far

	--build some planes
	self.innerPlanes = {}
	self.innerPlanes[1] = PlaneFromPoints(ra1, rc1, ra2) --near
	--planes[2] = PlaneFromPoints(rb1, rb2,rd1) --far 

	self.innerPlanes[2] = PlaneFromPoints(ra1,rb1,rc1) --top
	self.innerPlanes[3] = PlaneFromPoints(ra1,ra2,rb1) --left
	self.innerPlanes[4] = PlaneFromPoints(ra2,rc2,rb2)--bot
	self.innerPlanes[5] = PlaneFromPoints(rc1,rd1,rd2)  --right
		
	debug.profileend()
end

--in integers
function module:RenderDebugPixel(x, y, z)
	if (self.debugGui == nil) then
		return
	end
	local box = self.debugBox:Clone()
	box.Position = UDim2.new(0, x * self.yPixelSize, 0, y * self.yPixelSize)
	box.Parent = self.debugGui
	local zc =  1-math.clamp( z / 500  ,0,1)
	box.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(zc,zc,zc) 
	box.Visible = true
	
	table.insert(self.debugPixels, box)
end


function module:RenderDebugPixelRed(x, y, z)
	if (self.debugGui == nil) then
		return
	end
	local box = self.debugBox:Clone()
	box.Position = UDim2.new(0, x * self.yPixelSize, 0, y * self.yPixelSize)
	box.Parent = self.debugGui
	local zc =  1-math.clamp( z / 500  ,0,1)
	box.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1,0,0) 
	box.Visible = true

	table.insert(self.debugPixels, box)
end

local function PlotPixelForOccluder(x, y, z)
	local spot = x + (y * module.xCount)
	local existingZ = module.depthBuffer[spot] 
	
	if (existingZ ~= nil and existingZ < z) then
		return false
	end
		
	module.depthBuffer[spot] = z
	return false
end

local function TestPixel(x, y, z)
	numPixelsTested+=1
	local spot = x + (y* module.xCount)
	local existingZ = module.depthBuffer[spot] 
	
	--Visible
	if (existingZ == nil or existingZ >= z) then
		return true
	end

	return false
end


local function TestPixelDebug(x, y, z)
	numPixelsTested+=1
	local spot = x + (y* module.xCount)
	local existingZ = module.depthBuffer[spot] 

	--Visible
	if (existingZ == nil or existingZ >= z) then
		module.debugDepthBuffer[spot] = z
		return true
	end
	
	return false
end

local function CompareCFrames(a,b, oldSize, newSize)
	
	if (oldSize:FuzzyEq(newSize,0.01) == false) then
		return false
	end	
	
	local vecA = a.Position
	local vecB = b.Position
	if (vecA:FuzzyEq(vecB, 0.01) == false) then
		return false
	end
	
	if (a.UpVector:FuzzyEq(b.UpVector, 0.01) == false) then
		return false
	end
	
	return true
end

local function IsTriangleClockwise(A, B, C)
	local crossProduct = (B.X - A.X) * (C.Y - A.Y) - (C.X - A.X) * (B.Y - A.Y)
	return crossProduct < 0  -- Returns true if the cross product is negative (CW), false otherwise (CCW)
end
 
function module:RenderOccluders(camera)
	debug.profilebegin("RenderOcc")
	local startOcclusionTime = tick()
	
	self.depthBuffer = {}
	self.debugDepthBuffer = {}
	
	if (self.debugBox) then
		self.debugBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, self.yPixelSize, 0,  self.yPixelSize)
	end
		
	module.stats.transformedVerts = 0
	module.stats.occluderTriangles = 0
	module.stats.dynamicVisTriangles = 0
	module.stats.visibleDynamicVis = 0
	module.stats.totalDynamicVis =0
	
	local camPos = camera.CFrame.Position
	
	local occluders = collectionService:GetTagged("Occluder")
	 
	for key,value in occluders do
		
		local record = self.occluderRecords[value]
		if (record == nil) then
			record = {}
			record.originalParent = value.Parent
			record.dirty = true
			
			self.occluderRecords[value] = record
		end
		
		if (value:IsDescendantOf(game.Workspace) == false) then
			continue
		end
		local cf, size = self:GetBounds(value, record)

		if (record.lastCFrame == nil or CompareCFrames(record.lastCFrame,cf, record.lastSize, size) == false) then
			record.dirty = true
			record.lastCFrame = cf
			record.lastSize = size
		end		
		
		if (self:PointInsideBounds(camPos,cf,size) == true ) then
			continue
		end
			
		debug.profilebegin("GenTriangles")
		local screenSpaceTriangles, exteriorPolygon = self:GenerateTrianglesForOccluderClipped(record, value, camPos, cf, size, camera)
		debug.profileend()
				

		
		--draw it
		if (self.debugging == true) then
			local a = exteriorPolygon[#exteriorPolygon]
			for i=1, #exteriorPolygon do
				local b = exteriorPolygon[i]
				module:DebugLineScreenSpace(a,b, Color3.new(1,0,0), module.debugGui)
				a=b
			end
		end
				
		debug.profilebegin("FillTriangle")
		for _,triangle in screenSpaceTriangles do
			
			local screenSpaceVert1 = (triangle[1])
			local screenSpaceVert2 = (triangle[2])
			local screenSpaceVert3 = (triangle[3])
			
			local tri  = 
			{
				Vector3.new(screenSpaceVert1.x / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert1.y / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert1.z),
				Vector3.new(screenSpaceVert2.x / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert2.y / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert2.z),
				Vector3.new(screenSpaceVert3.x / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert3.y / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert3.z)
			}
			
			module.stats.transformedVerts+=3
			module.stats.occluderTriangles += 1
			
			debug.profilebegin("Fill")
			triangleFill:TriangleFillSpecial(tri, exteriorPolygon, self.yPixelSize, PlotPixelForOccluder)
			debug.profileend()
		end
		debug.profileend()
	end
	
	if (self.drawDebugText) then
		table.insert(self.occlusionTime, tick() - startOcclusionTime)
	end
	debug.profileend()
	
	debug.profilebegin("CheckDynamicVis")
	
	--3.6, 3.01
	local startCheckDynamicVisTime = tick()
	
	local dynamicVis = collectionService:GetTagged("DynamicVis")
	
	local theTime = tick()
		
	for key,value in dynamicVis do
				
		local record = self.dynamicVisRecords[value]
		if (record == nil) then
			record = {}
			record.nextAllowedHideTime = theTime + 1
			record.visible = true
			record.originalParent = value.Parent
			record.dirty = true
			record.desireVisible = true
			record.checkTime = 0
			
			self.dynamicVisRecords[value] = record
		end
 
		--hacky, but these can load in later.
		if (record.shadowCaster == nil and theTime > record.checkTime) then
			record.checkTime = theTime + 1
		
			--Shadowcasters get placed back into the scene when a model gets occluded, so it still casts a reasonable shadow
			local shadowCaster = value:FindFirstChild("ShadowCaster")
			if (shadowCaster) then
				record.shadowCaster = shadowCaster
				record.shadowCaster.Parent = nil
			end
		end

		local cf, size = self:GetBounds(value, record)
		
		--See if the dynamic vis object has moved
		if (record.lastCFrame == nil or CompareCFrames(record.lastCFrame,cf, record.lastSize, size) == false) then
			record.dirty = true
			record.lastCFrame = cf
			record.lastSize = size
		end
		
		if (self:IsBoundingBoxVisible(self.planes, cf, size) == false) then		
			
			--not in frustum, skip the rest of this
			
			--Don't assume its visible, leave it however it was
			--record.desireVisible = true
			continue
		end
		
		if (self.override == true) then
			record.desireVisible = true
			continue
		end
		
		--we're in view, do more tests
		self.stats.totalDynamicVis+=1
		if (record.visible == true) then
			module.stats.visibleDynamicVis +=1
		end
		
		--Skip the check if we're visible, but not allowed to hide yet
		if (record.visible == true and theTime < record.nextAllowedHideTime) then
			record.desireVisible = true
			continue
		end
				
		--Skip the check if we're inside the object
		if (self:PointInsideBounds(camPos,cf,size) == true) then
			record.desireVisible = true
			continue
		end
		
		local func = TestPixel
		if (module.debugging == true) then
			func = TestPixelDebug
		end
		
		--Do a fast check
		if (record.visible == false) then
			local screenPoint = self:IsPointVisible(cf.Position, camera, func)
	
			if (screenPoint == true) then 
				record.desireVisible = true
				continue
			end
		end
		
		--Do the full check
		local triangles, anyClipping = self:GenerateTrianglesForTester(record, value, camPos, cf, size)
		
		if (#triangles == 0) then
			--All the triangles were clipped, keep whatever status it had
			continue
		end
		
		local cancelled = false
 		numPixelsTested = 0
		
		local cache = {}
		
		for _,triangle in triangles do

			local tri = {}

			local vert = triangle[1]
			local screenSpaceVert1 = cache[vert]
			if (screenSpaceVert1 == nil) then
				screenSpaceVert1 = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(triangle[1])
				screenSpaceVert1 = Vector3.new(screenSpaceVert1.x / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert1.y / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert1.z)
				cache[vert] = screenSpaceVert1
			end
			
			local vert = triangle[2]
			local screenSpaceVert2 = cache[vert]
			if (screenSpaceVert2 == nil) then
				screenSpaceVert2 = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(triangle[2])
				screenSpaceVert2 = Vector3.new(screenSpaceVert2.x / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert2.y / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert2.z)
				cache[vert] = screenSpaceVert2
			end

			local vert = triangle[3]
			local screenSpaceVert3 = cache[vert]
			if (screenSpaceVert3 == nil) then
				screenSpaceVert3 = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(triangle[3])
				screenSpaceVert3 = Vector3.new(screenSpaceVert3.x / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert3.y / self.yPixelSize, screenSpaceVert3.z)
				cache[vert] = screenSpaceVert3
			end
			
			local tri = {screenSpaceVert1, screenSpaceVert2, screenSpaceVert3 }
			
			module.stats.transformedVerts += 3
			module.stats.dynamicVisTriangles += 1
			
			local res = triangleFill:TriangleFill(tri, func)
			
			if (res == true) then
				--Some of it was visible	
				cancelled = true
				break
			end
		end
		
		--Vis test completed...
		--All the pixels we tried to render failed their Ztest
		if (cancelled == false) then
			
			--Triangles were too thin to test, assume the object is fine however it was
			if (numPixelsTested == 0) then
				continue
			end
			
			--100% sure we cant see this thing			
			record.desireVisible = false
			continue
		end
		
		
		
		--Absolutely last chance test to remove it - small bounding boxes with no pixels, check the center pixel
		--But only do this if the polygon is completely on screen
		if (numPixelsTested == 0 and anyClipping == false) then
			local screenPoint = self:IsPointVisible(cf.Position, camera, func)

			if (screenPoint == false) then 
				record.desireVisible = false
				continue
			end
		end
		
		--Made it all the way here, it should be onscreen
		record.desireVisible = true
		local tris = #triangles
	end
	
	self:UpdateVisibility()
	
	if (self.drawDebugText) then
		table.insert(self.checkDynamicVisTime, tick() - startCheckDynamicVisTime)
	end
	debug.profileend()
end

function module:TestSquareBounds(minx, maxx, miny, maxy, func)
	--these are in pixel space, convert them to tile space
	minx=math.floor(minx / self.yPixelSize)
	miny=math.floor(miny / self.yPixelSize)
	maxx=math.ceil(maxx / self.yPixelSize)
	maxy=math.ceil(maxy / self.yPixelSize)
	
	for x=minx, maxx do
		for y = miny, maxy do
		--	if (func())
		end
	end
end

function module:DrawOccludedBoundingBox()
	if (self.debugging == false) then
		return
	end
	local camera = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera
	local camPos = camera.CFrame.Position 	
	for value,record in self.dynamicVisRecords do
		
		if (typeof(value) == "string") then
			continue
		end
	 
		if (record.visible == true) then
			continue
		end	
	 			
		--Draw in a bounding box
		--Transform the triangles into screenspace
		local cf, size = self:GetBounds(value, record)
		local list  = {}
		local triangles = self:GenerateTrianglesForTester(record, value, camPos, cf, size)
		for _,triangle in triangles do
			triangle[1] = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(triangle[1])
			triangle[2] = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(triangle[2])
			triangle[3] = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(triangle[3])

			table.insert(list, triangle[1])
			table.insert(list, triangle[2])
			table.insert(list, triangle[3])
		end
	 		
		local exteriorPolygon = convexHull:MakeConvexHull(list)
					
		local col = value:GetAttribute("boxcolor") or Color3.new(0,0,1)
		local a = exteriorPolygon[#exteriorPolygon]
		for i=1, #exteriorPolygon do
			local b = exteriorPolygon[i]
			module:DebugLineScreenSpace(a,b, col, module.debugGui)
			a=b
		end
		
		--center tick
		local screenSpaceVert1 = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(cf.Position) 
		local screenSpaceVert2 = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(cf.Position + Vector3.new(0,1,0)) 
		--module:DebugLineScreenSpace(screenSpaceVert1,screenSpaceVert2, Color3.new(1,1,0), module.debugGui)
	end
end
 

function module:UpdateVisibility()
	debug.profilebegin("UpdateParents")	
	local dynamicVis = collectionService:GetTagged("DynamicVis")
	for key, value in dynamicVis do
		local record = self.dynamicVisRecords[value]
		
		if (record.desireVisible == true) then

			if (record.visible == false) then
				--Make Visible
				value.Parent = record.originalParent
				record.visible = true
				record.nextAllowedHideTime = tick() + 1
				
				--Hide the shadowcasters 
				if (record.shadowCaster) then
					record.shadowCaster.Parent = nil
				end
				
			end
		else
			if (record.visible == true) then
				--Hide the object
				value.Parent = game.Lighting
				record.visible = false
				
				--Sub in the the shadowcasters 
				if (record.shadowCaster) then
					record.shadowCaster.Parent = record.originalParent
				end
			end
		end
	end
	debug.profileend()
end

function module:Print(str,color)
	local text = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	text.AutoLocalize = false
	text.Text = str
	text.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	text.TextSize = 8
	text.TextColor3 = color or Color3.new(0.94902, 1, 0)
	text.Position = UDim2.new(0,10, 0, self.debugTextPos)
	self.debugTextPos+=16
	text.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	text.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Bottom	
	text.Parent = self.debugGui

	table.insert(self.debugTris, text)
end

local function format(num)
	local num = math.floor(num * 10000)
	num/=10
	if (num<0.1) then
		return "0.0"
	else
		return tostring(num)
	end
end

function module:PrintStats()
	self.occlusionTimeAvg = 0
	if (#self.occlusionTime > 0) then
		for _,v in self.occlusionTime do
			self.occlusionTimeAvg += v
		end
		self.occlusionTimeAvg /= #self.occlusionTime
		while (#self.occlusionTime > 60) do
			table.remove(self.occlusionTime,1)
		end
	end
	
	self.checkDynamicVisTimeAvg = 0
	if (#self.checkDynamicVisTime > 0) then
		for _,v in self.checkDynamicVisTime do
			self.checkDynamicVisTimeAvg += v
		end
		self.checkDynamicVisTimeAvg /= #self.checkDynamicVisTime
		while (#self.checkDynamicVisTime > 60) do
			table.remove(self.checkDynamicVisTime,1)
		end
	end
	
	self.debugTextPos = 156
	self:Print("Dynamic Objects Culled: " .. "(" .. self.stats.totalDynamicVis - self.stats.visibleDynamicVis .. " of ".. self.stats.totalDynamicVis .. ")" )
	self:Print("Occluder time:" .. format(self.occlusionTimeAvg) .. "ms")
	self:Print("DynamicVis time:" .. format(self.checkDynamicVisTimeAvg) .. "ms")
	
	self:Print("OccluderTriangles: " .. self.stats.occluderTriangles)
	self:Print("DynamicVisTriangles: " .. self.stats.dynamicVisTriangles)
	self:Print("TransformedVerts: " .. self.stats.transformedVerts)
	
	self:Print("")
		
	local w = Color3.new(1,1,1)
	self:Print("F5 to toggle software occlusion debug view", w)
	self:Print("Hold F6 to supress occlusion", w)
	self:Print("Hold F7 to supress details", w)
	self:Print("Shift+F2 for roblox render stats", w)
	self:Print("F8 to toggle this text", w)
end

function module:GetCenter(part)
	if (part:IsA("BasePart")) then
		return part.Position	
	end
	return part.WorldPivot.p
end

function module:IsPointVisible(pos,camera, testPixelFunc)
	local vert = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(pos)
	
	if (vert.z < 0) then
		return false
	end
	
	local x = math.floor(vert.x / self.yPixelSize)
	local y = math.floor(vert.y / self.yPixelSize)
	if (x < 0 or x >= module.xCount) then
		return false
	end
	if (y < 0 or y >= module.yCount) then
		return false
	end
	
	return testPixelFunc(x, y, vert.z)
end

function module:GetBounds(part, record)
	
	if (record.modelType == nil) then
		if (part:IsA("BasePart")) then
			record.modelType = 0
		elseif(part:IsA("Model")) then
			record.modelType = 1
		else
			record.modelType = 2
		end
	end


	if (record.modelType == 0) then
		return part.CFrame, part.Size
	elseif (record.modelType == 1) then
		return part:GetBoundingBox()
	end
	return nil
end

function module:GetBoundsCached(part, record)

	if (record.modelType == nil) then
		if (part:IsA("BasePart")) then
			record.modelType = 0
		elseif(part:IsA("Model")) then
			record.modelType = 1
		else
			record.modelType = 2
		end
	end
	
	

	local cf = nil
	local size = nil

	if (record.modelType == 0) then

		return part.CFrame, part.size 
	elseif (record.modelType == 1) then
		
		if (record.cf == nil) then
			record.cf, record.size = part:GetBoundingBox()
		end
		
		return record.cf, record.size
	end
	return nil
end

function module:PointInsideBounds(pos, cf, size)
	local testPos = cf:PointToObjectSpace(pos)
	size/=2
	
	if (testPos.x < -size.x or testPos.x > size.x) then
		return false
	end
	if (testPos.y < -size.y or testPos.y > size.y) then
		return false
	end
	if (testPos.z < -size.z or testPos.z > size.z) then
		return false
	end
	return true
end

 
function module:GenerateTrianglesForOccluderClipped(record, part, camPos, cf, size, camera)
	local counter = 1

	--Todo: Optimize this away using dirty flags on the transform
	if (record.dirty == true) then

		record.transformedCorners = {}
		for key,corner in corners do
			local pos = cf * ( corner * size )
			table.insert(record.transformedCorners, pos)
		end
		record.dirty = false
	end

	local tris = {}

	local outerPlanes = {}
	local pos = camPos
	local transformedCorners = record.transformedCorners

	--If we're using boxes, then only the +X side or X- side is facing the camera, so we can skip emitting the backface triangles 
	--X+
	if (self:TestVisPoint(pos,transformedCorners[6], transformedCorners[8], transformedCorners[4])) then
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[6], transformedCorners[8], transformedCorners[4]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[2], transformedCorners[6]} )
	else
		--x-
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[3], transformedCorners[7]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[7], transformedCorners[5]} )
	end

	if (self:TestVisPoint(pos, transformedCorners[3], transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[7])) then
		--y+
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[3], transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[7]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[7], transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[8]} )
	else
		--y-
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[5], transformedCorners[6], transformedCorners[2]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[5], transformedCorners[2], transformedCorners[1]} )
	end

	if (self:TestVisPoint(pos,transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[2], transformedCorners[4])) then
		--z+
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[2], transformedCorners[4]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[3]} )
	else
		--z-
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[5], transformedCorners[7], transformedCorners[8]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[5], transformedCorners[8], transformedCorners[6]} )
	end


	--Draw the raw triangles in
	if (module.debugging == true and false) then
		for key,tri in tris do
			module:DebugLine(tri[1], tri[2], 0.3, Color3.new(1,0,0),0.5)
			module:DebugLine(tri[2], tri[3], 0.3, Color3.new(1,0,0),0.5)
			module:DebugLine(tri[3], tri[1], 0.3, Color3.new(0,1,0),0.5)
		end
	end	


	--slightly clever pingpong system to pass the tris along to the next plane clip	
	local finalTris = tris
	for _,plane in self.outerPlanes do

		local newTris = {}
		for key,tri in finalTris do
			self:ClipTriangleToPlane(tri, plane, newTris)
		end
	
		
		if (#newTris == 0) then
			return {},{}
		
		end
		finalTris = newTris
	end 
	
	
	--Transform the triangles into screenspace
	local list = {}
	local cache = {} --skip transforms
	for _,triangle in finalTris do
		
		local vec = triangle[1]
		local a = cache[vec] 
		if (a == nil) then
			a =  camera:WorldToViewportPoint(vec)
			cache[vec] = a
		end
		table.insert(list, a)
		triangle[1] = a
				
		local vec = triangle[2]
		local a = cache[vec] 
		if (a == nil) then
			a = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(vec)
			cache[vec] = a
		end
		table.insert(list, a)
		triangle[2] = a
		
		local vec = triangle[3]
		local a = cache[vec] 
		if (a == nil) then
			a = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(vec)
			cache[vec] = a
		end
		table.insert(list, a)
		triangle[3] = a

		
	end
	
	local exteriorPolygon = convexHull:MakeConvexHull(list)
	
	return finalTris, exteriorPolygon
end

function module:GenerateTrianglesForTester(record, part, camPos, cf, size)
	local counter = 1

	--Todo: Optimize this away using dirty flags on the transform
	if (record.dirty == true) then
		
		record.transformedCorners = {}
		for key,corner in corners do
			local pos = cf * ( corner * size )
			table.insert(record.transformedCorners, pos)
		end
		record.dirty = false
	end
	
	local transformedCorners = record.transformedCorners
	local tris = {}
	local pos = camPos

	--If we're using boxes, then only the +X side or X- side is facing the camera, so we can skip emitting the backface triangles 
	--X+
	if (self:TestVisPoint(pos,transformedCorners[6], transformedCorners[8], transformedCorners[4])) then
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[6], transformedCorners[8], transformedCorners[4]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[2], transformedCorners[6]} )
	else
		--x-
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[3], transformedCorners[7]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[7], transformedCorners[5]} )
	end

	if (self:TestVisPoint(pos, transformedCorners[3], transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[7])) then
		--y+
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[3], transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[7]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[7], transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[8]} )
	else
		--y-
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[5], transformedCorners[6], transformedCorners[2]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[5], transformedCorners[2], transformedCorners[1]} )
	end

	if (self:TestVisPoint(pos,transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[2], transformedCorners[4])) then
		--z+
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[2], transformedCorners[4]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[1], transformedCorners[4], transformedCorners[3]} )
	else
		--z-
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[5], transformedCorners[7], transformedCorners[8]} )
		table.insert(tris, { transformedCorners[5], transformedCorners[8], transformedCorners[6]} )
	end

	--slightly clever pingpong system to pass the tris along to the next plane clip	
	local finalTris = tris
	local anyClipping = false
	for _,plane in self.innerPlanes do

		local newTris = {}

		for key,tri in finalTris do
			local clipped = self:ClipTriangleToPlane(tri, plane, newTris)
			if (clipped) then
				anyClipping = true
			end
		end

		finalTris = newTris
	end 

	return finalTris, anyClipping
end

function module:TestVisPoint(camPos, a,b,c)
	local viewVec = a-camPos
	
	local norm = (c-a):Cross(b-a)
	
	if (norm:Dot(viewVec) < 0) then
		return true
	end
	
	return false
end

function module:DebugLine(startPos, endPos, thickness,color, transparency)
	--create a debug line
	local part = Instance.new("Part")
	part.Shape = Enum.PartType.Block
	part.Size = Vector3.new(thickness,thickness,(startPos-endPos).Magnitude)
	part.Anchored = true
	part.CanCollide = false
	part.CanTouch = false
	part.CanQuery = false
	part.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
	part.Color = color
	part.Transparency = transparency
	
	local midPoint = (startPos+endPos) * 0.5
	local lookAtCFrame = CFrame.lookAt(midPoint,endPos) 
	part.CFrame = lookAtCFrame
	part.Parent = game.Workspace
	table.insert(self.debugTris,part)
end

function module:DebugLineScreenSpace(startPos, endPos, color, parentGui)
	startPos = Vector3.new(startPos.x, startPos.y,0)
	endPos = Vector3.new(endPos.x, endPos.y,0)
	-- Create the Frame instance
	local line = Instance.new("Frame")
	line.BorderSizePixel = 0
	line.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5,0.5)
	line.BackgroundColor3 = color or Color3.new(1, 1, 1) -- Default to white if no color is provided
	line.Parent = parentGui or game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui -- Default to PlayerGui if no parentGui is provided

	-- Calculate the length, midpoint, and rotation angle of the line
	local length = (endPos - startPos).Magnitude
	local midPoint = (startPos + endPos) / 2
	local rotationAngle = math.deg(math.atan2((endPos.Y - startPos.Y), endPos.X - startPos.X))

	-- Set the size and position of the Frame
	line.Size = UDim2.new(0, length, 0, 2)
	line.Position = UDim2.new(0, midPoint.X, 0, midPoint.Y)

	-- Rotate the Frame to create the line
	line.Rotation = rotationAngle
	table.insert(self.debugTris,line)

	return line
end

function module:DebugBall(pos)
	local col = self.colors[(#self.debugTris % 1000)  + 1]
	local part = Instance.new("Part")
	part.Shape= Enum.PartType.Ball
	part.Size = Vector3.new(1,1,1)
	part.Anchored = true
	part.CanCollide = false
	part.CanTouch = false
	part.CanQuery = false
	part.Position = pos
	part.Color = col
	part.Parent = game.Workspace
	table.insert(self.debugTris,part)
end

function module:DistanceToPlane(point, plane)
	return plane.n:Dot(point) + plane.d
end

--todo: this can be mildly optimized by grouping some of the tests (ad < 0 etc)
function module:ClipTriangleToPlane(tri , plane, tris)
	local a = tri[1] 
	local b = tri[2]
	local c = tri[3]
	
	local ad = plane.n:Dot(a) + plane.d
	local bd = plane.n:Dot(b) + plane.d
	local cd = plane.n:Dot(c) + plane.d
		
	--Is entirely offscreen, cull	
	if (ad < 0 and bd < 0 and cd < 0) then
		return true
	end 
	
	--is entirely onscreen
	if (ad >= 0 and bd >=0 and cd >= 0) then
		table.insert(tris, tri)
		return false
	end
	
	--figure out which parts of the triangle to keep
	if (ad < 0 and bd > 0 and cd > 0) then
		
		-- out
		--    |   b
		-- a  |	 
		--    |   c
				
		local abn = (b-a).Unit
		local acn = (c-a).Unit
		local intersectA = self:RayPlane(a, abn, plane.n, plane.d)
		local intersectB = self:RayPlane(a, acn, plane.n, plane.d)
		
		local triA = {intersectA, b, c}
		local triB = {intersectB, intersectA, c}
 
		table.insert(tris, triA)	
		table.insert(tris, triB)
	 
		return true	
	end
	
	if (bd < 0 and cd > 0 and ad > 0) then

		-- out
		--    |   c
		-- b  |	 
		--    |   a

		local bcn = (c-b).Unit
		local ban = (a-b).Unit
		local intersectA = self:RayPlane(b, bcn, plane.n, plane.d)
		local intersectB = self:RayPlane(b, ban, plane.n, plane.d)
		
		local triA = {intersectA, c, a}
		local triB = {intersectB, intersectA, a}
 
		table.insert(tris, triA)	
		table.insert(tris, triB)
  
		return true	
	end
		
	if (cd < 0 and ad > 0 and bd > 0) then

		-- out
		--    |   a
		-- c  |	 
		--    |   b

		local can = (a-c).Unit
		local cbn = (b-c).Unit
		local intersectA = self:RayPlane(c, can, plane.n, plane.d)
		local intersectB = self:RayPlane(c, cbn, plane.n, plane.d)

		local triA = {intersectA, a, b}
		local triB = {intersectB, intersectA, b}
 
		table.insert(tris, triA)	
		table.insert(tris, triB)
 
		return true	
	end

	if (ad > 0 and bd < 0 and cd < 0) then

		-- in
		--    |   b
		-- a  |	 
		--    |   c

		local abn = (b-a).Unit
		local acn = (c-a).Unit
		local intersectA = self:RayPlane(a, abn, plane.n, plane.d)
		local intersectB = self:RayPlane(a, acn, plane.n, plane.d)

		local triA = {a , intersectA, intersectB}

		table.insert(tris, triA)	
		
		return 1
	end
 
	if (bd > 0 and cd < 0 and ad < 0) then

		-- in
		--    |   c
		-- b  |	 
		--    |   a

		local bcn = (c-b).Unit
		local ban = (a-b).Unit
		local intersectA = self:RayPlane(b, bcn, plane.n, plane.d)
		local intersectB = self:RayPlane(b, ban, plane.n, plane.d)

		local triA = {b, intersectA, intersectB}
	 
		table.insert(tris, triA)	
	 
		return true	
	end

	if (cd > 0 and ad < 0 and bd < 0) then

		-- in
		--    |   a
		-- c  |	 
		--    |   b

		local can = (a-c).Unit
		local cbn = (b-c).Unit
		local intersectA = self:RayPlane(c, can, plane.n, plane.d)
		local intersectB = self:RayPlane(c, cbn, plane.n, plane.d)

		local triA = {c, intersectA, intersectB}
		
		table.insert(tris, triA)	
	  
		return true	
	end

	return true
end

--abbreviated ray plane when you know that it'll always intesect
function module:RayPlane(rayOrigin, rayDirection, planeNormal, planeDistance)
	local vdot = rayDirection:Dot(planeNormal)
	local ndot = -rayOrigin:Dot(planeNormal) - planeDistance

--	if (Mathf.Approximately(vdot, 0.0f))
--		{
--			enter = 0.0F;
--			return false;
--}

	local t = ndot / vdot
	return rayOrigin + rayDirection * t
end

function module:SphereVisible(planes, worldPoint, radius)
	for j = 1,6 do
		local dist = worldPoint:Dot(planes[j].n) + planes[j].d + radius
		if(dist < 0) then
			return false 
		end
	end

	return true
end

function module:IsBoundingBoxVisible(planes, cframe, size)
	local halfSize = size / 2
	
	--[[  
	local corners = {
		cframe:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(halfSize.X, halfSize.Y, halfSize.Z)),
		cframe:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(-halfSize.X, halfSize.Y, halfSize.Z)),
		cframe:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(halfSize.X, -halfSize.Y, halfSize.Z)),
		cframe:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(-halfSize.X, -halfSize.Y, halfSize.Z)),
		cframe:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(halfSize.X, halfSize.Y, -halfSize.Z)),
		cframe:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(-halfSize.X, halfSize.Y, -halfSize.Z)),
		cframe:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(halfSize.X, -halfSize.Y, -halfSize.Z)),
		cframe:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(-halfSize.X, -halfSize.Y, -halfSize.Z))
	}]]--
	 
	local corners = 
	{
		cframe:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(halfSize.X, halfSize.Y, halfSize.Z), 
		Vector3.new(-halfSize.X, halfSize.Y, halfSize.Z),
		Vector3.new(halfSize.X, -halfSize.Y, halfSize.Z),
		Vector3.new(-halfSize.X, -halfSize.Y, halfSize.Z),
		Vector3.new(halfSize.X, halfSize.Y, -halfSize.Z),
		Vector3.new(-halfSize.X, halfSize.Y, -halfSize.Z),
		Vector3.new(halfSize.X, -halfSize.Y, -halfSize.Z),
		Vector3.new(-halfSize.X, -halfSize.Y, -halfSize.Z))
	} 

	for _,plane in planes do
		local isAnyCornerVisible = false

		for i = 1, 8 do
			local corner = corners[i]
			local d = plane.n:Dot(corner) + plane.d

			if d >= 0 then
				isAnyCornerVisible = true
				break
			end
		end

		if not isAnyCornerVisible then
			return false
		end
	end

	return true
end


function module:Setup()
	self:InitColors()
	local userInput = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	
	if (module.allowDebug) then
		userInput.InputBegan:Connect(function(inputObject)
			if (inputObject.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard) then
				if (inputObject.KeyCode==Enum.KeyCode.F8) then
					self.drawDebugText = not self.drawDebugText
				end
				if (inputObject.KeyCode==Enum.KeyCode.F6) then

					self.override = true
				end
				if (inputObject.KeyCode==Enum.KeyCode.F5) then

					self.debugging =not self.debugging
				end
			end

		end)

		userInput.InputEnded:Connect(function(inputObject)
			if (inputObject.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard) then
				if (inputObject.KeyCode==Enum.KeyCode.F6) then
					self.override = false
				end
			end
		end)
	end
	
	game["Run Service"].Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		module:Update()
	end)
end

module:Setup()

return module

--[[
    ConvexHull (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3 → RobloxVisToolsReplicatedFirst → DynamicVisClient
    Parent: DynamicVisClient
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:32

--!native
local module = {}

function ccw(a,b,c)
	
	return (b.x - a.x) * (c.y - a.y) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x) > 0 
end

function pop_back(ta)
	table.remove(ta,#ta)
	return ta
end

function inside(p, cp1, cp2)
	return (cp2.x-cp1.x)*(p.y-cp1.y) > (cp2.y-cp1.y)*(p.x-cp1.x)
end
function outside(p, cp1, cp2)
	return (cp2.x-cp1.x)*(p.y-cp1.y) < (cp2.y-cp1.y)*(p.x-cp1.x)
end

function intersection(cp1, cp2, s, e)
	local dcx, dcy = cp1.x-cp2.x, cp1.y-cp2.y
	local dpx, dpy = s.x-e.x, s.y-e.y
	local n1 = cp1.x*cp2.y - cp1.y*cp2.x
	local n2 = s.x*e.y - s.y*e.x
	local n3 = 1 / (dcx*dpy - dcy*dpx)
	local x = (n1*dpx - n2*dcx) * n3
	local y = (n1*dpy - n2*dcy) * n3
	return Vector2.new(x,y)
end

function module:MakeConvexHull(points)

	table.sort(points, function(left, right)
		local tolerance = 1e-6  
		if math.abs(left.x - right.x) < tolerance then
			return left.y < right.y
		else
			return left.x < right.x
		end
	end)

	local h = {}

	-- lower hull
	for i,pt in points do
		while #h >= 2 and not ccw(h[#h-1], h[#h], pt) do
			table.remove(h,#h)
		end
		table.insert(h,pt)
	end

	-- upper hull
	local t = #h + 1
	for i=#points, 1, -1 do
		local pt = points[i]
		while #h >= t and not ccw(h[#h-1], h[#h], pt) do
			table.remove(h,#h)
		end
		table.insert(h,pt)
	end

	table.remove(h,#h)
	return h
end

return module

    TriangleFill (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3 → RobloxVisToolsReplicatedFirst → DynamicVisClient

--!native
local module = {}

local function PlotPixel(x,y,z)
end

module.PlotPixel = PlotPixel

local function makeGradients(triangle)
	local res = {}

	local OneOverdX = 1 /(((triangle[2].X - triangle[3].X) *	(triangle[1].Y - triangle[3].Y)) -	((triangle[1].X - triangle[3].X) * 	(triangle[2].Y - triangle[3].Y)))
	local OneOverdY = -OneOverdX

	res.aOneOverZ = {}
	res.aOneOverZ[1] = 1 / triangle[1].Z
	res.aOneOverZ[2] = 1 / triangle[2].Z
	res.aOneOverZ[3] = 1 / triangle[3].Z

	res.dOneOverZdX = OneOverdX * (((res.aOneOverZ[2] - res.aOneOverZ[3]) *	(triangle[1].Y - triangle[3].Y)) - ((res.aOneOverZ[1] - res.aOneOverZ[3]) *	(triangle[2].Y - triangle[3].Y)))
	res.dOneOverZdY = OneOverdY * (((res.aOneOverZ[2] - res.aOneOverZ[3]) *	(triangle[1].X - triangle[3].X)) - ((res.aOneOverZ[1] - res.aOneOverZ[3]) *	(triangle[2].X - triangle[3].X)))

	return res
end

local function makeEdge(gradients, triangle, top, bottom)
	local res = {}

	res.Y = math.ceil(triangle[top].Y)
	local yEnd = math.ceil(triangle[bottom].Y)

	res.height = yEnd - res.Y

	local YPrestep = res.Y - triangle[top].Y

	local RealHeight = triangle[bottom].Y - triangle[top].Y
	local RealWidth = triangle[bottom].X - triangle[top].X

	res.X = ((RealWidth * YPrestep)/RealHeight) + triangle[top].X

	res.XStep = RealWidth/RealHeight

	local XPrestep = res.X - triangle[top].X

	res.OneOverZ = gradients.aOneOverZ[top] +	YPrestep * gradients.dOneOverZdY + XPrestep * gradients.dOneOverZdX
	res.OneOverZStep = res.XStep * gradients.dOneOverZdX + gradients.dOneOverZdY
	return res
end

local function step(edge)
	edge.X += edge.XStep
	edge.Y+=1
	edge.height-=1
	edge.OneOverZ += edge.OneOverZStep

end

function drawScanLine(gradients, pLeft, pRight)
	local XStart = math.ceil(pLeft.X)
	local XPrestep = XStart - pLeft.X

	--pDestBits += pLeft->Y * DestWidthBytes + XStart;

	local width = math.ceil(pRight.X) - XStart

	local OneOverZ = pLeft.OneOverZ +	XPrestep * gradients.dOneOverZdX

	local x = XStart
	local y = pLeft.Y
	
	while(width > 0) do
		width -= 1

		local z = 1 / OneOverZ --z is perspective correct 
		local cancelled = module.PlotPixel(x, y, z)
		if (cancelled) then
			return true
		end
		x+=1
		OneOverZ += gradients.dOneOverZdX
	end
	return false
end
 
function IsPointInsidePolygon(point, polygon)
	local n = #polygon
	local inside = false
	local p1 = polygon[n]
	local p2

	for i = 1, n do
		p2 = polygon[i]
		if ((p2.y > point.y) ~= (p1.y > point.y)) and
			(point.x < (p1.x - p2.x) * (point.y - p2.y) / (p1.y - p2.y) + p2.x) then
			inside = not inside
		end
		p1 = p2
	end
 
	return inside
end

--Same but no cancel possible
function drawScanLineForOccluder(gradients, pLeft, pRight, polygon, pixelSize, halfPixelSize)
	local XStart = math.ceil(pLeft.X)
	local XPrestep = XStart - pLeft.X

	--pDestBits += pLeft->Y * DestWidthBytes + XStart;

	local width = math.ceil(pRight.X) - XStart

	local OneOverZ = pLeft.OneOverZ +	XPrestep * gradients.dOneOverZdX

	local x = XStart
	local y = pLeft.Y
	
	local isLeftSideIn = false
	
	
	--Todo: we can calculate the right hand side in a loop in advance
	if (width > 0) then
		while(width > 0) do
			
			if (isLeftSideIn == false) then
				if (IsPointInsidePolygon(Vector3.new( (x * pixelSize) - halfPixelSize, (y * pixelSize) - halfPixelSize,0),polygon) and IsPointInsidePolygon( Vector3.new( (x * pixelSize) - halfPixelSize, (y * pixelSize) + halfPixelSize,0),polygon)) then
					isLeftSideIn = true
				end
			end
			--Start checking the right side once we've established the left side is in			
			if (isLeftSideIn == true) then
				local topRight = Vector3.new( (x * pixelSize) + halfPixelSize, (y * pixelSize) - halfPixelSize,0)
				if (IsPointInsidePolygon(topRight,polygon) == false) then
					--all done 
					return
				end
				local botRight = Vector3.new( (x * pixelSize) + halfPixelSize, (y * pixelSize) + halfPixelSize,0)
				if (IsPointInsidePolygon(botRight,polygon) == false) then
					--all done 
					return
				end
			end
			
			if (isLeftSideIn == true) then
				local z = 1 / OneOverZ --z is perspective correct 
				module.PlotPixel(x, y, z)
			end
			
			width -= 1
			x+=1
			OneOverZ += gradients.dOneOverZdX
		end
	end
	return false
end



function module:TriangleFill(triangle, procedure)
	module.PlotPixel = procedure

	local Y0 = triangle[1].y
	local Y1 = triangle[2].y
	local Y2 = triangle[3].y

	local Top,Middle, Bottom, MiddleCompare, BottomCompare


	if(Y0 < Y1) then
		if(Y2 < Y0) then
			Top = 3 
			Middle = 1
			Bottom = 2
			MiddleCompare = 0
			BottomCompare = 1
		else
			Top = 1
			if(Y1 < Y2) then
				Middle = 2 
				Bottom = 3
				MiddleCompare = 1 
				BottomCompare = 2
			else
				Middle = 3 
				Bottom = 2
				MiddleCompare = 2
				BottomCompare = 1
			end
		end
	elseif (Y2 < Y1) then
		Top = 3 
		Middle = 2 
		Bottom = 1
		MiddleCompare = 1
		BottomCompare = 0
	else
		Top = 2
		if(Y0 < Y2) then
			Middle = 1 
			Bottom = 3
			MiddleCompare = 3 
			BottomCompare = 2
		else 
			Middle = 3
			Bottom = 1
			MiddleCompare = 2
			BottomCompare = 3
		end
	end

	local gradients = makeGradients(triangle)
	local topToBottom = makeEdge(gradients,triangle, Top, Bottom)
	local topToMiddle = makeEdge(gradients,triangle, Top, Middle)
	local middleToBottom = makeEdge(gradients,triangle, Middle, Bottom)
	local middleIsLeft = true
	local pLeft,pRight

	if (BottomCompare > MiddleCompare) then
		middleIsLeft = false
		pLeft = topToBottom
		pRight = topToMiddle
	else
		middleIsLeft = true
		pLeft = topToMiddle
		pRight = topToBottom
	end

	local height = topToMiddle.height
	while(height > 0) do
		height-=1
		local cancelled = drawScanLine(gradients,pLeft,pRight)
		if (cancelled == true) then
			return true
		end
		step(topToMiddle)
		step(topToBottom)
	end

	height = middleToBottom.height

	if (middleIsLeft)  then
		pLeft = middleToBottom
		pRight = topToBottom
	else 
		pLeft = topToBottom
		pRight = middleToBottom
	end

	while(height > 0) do
		height-=1
		local cancelled = drawScanLine(gradients,pLeft,pRight)
		if (cancelled == true) then
			return true
		end
		step(middleToBottom) 
		step(topToBottom)		
	end

	return false
end

--For occluders
function module:TriangleFillSpecial(triangle, polygon, pixelSize, procedure)
	module.PlotPixel = procedure
	
	local Y0 = triangle[1].y
	local Y1 = triangle[2].y
	local Y2 = triangle[3].y

	local Top,Middle, Bottom, MiddleCompare, BottomCompare

	if(Y0 < Y1) then
		if(Y2 < Y0) then
			Top = 3 
			Middle = 1
			Bottom = 2
			MiddleCompare = 0
			BottomCompare = 1
		else
			Top = 1
			if(Y1 < Y2) then
				Middle = 2 
				Bottom = 3
				MiddleCompare = 1 
				BottomCompare = 2
			else
				Middle = 3 
				Bottom = 2
				MiddleCompare = 2
				BottomCompare = 1
			end
		end
	elseif (Y2 < Y1) then
		Top = 3 
		Middle = 2 
		Bottom = 1
		MiddleCompare = 1
		BottomCompare = 0
	else
		Top = 2
		if(Y0 < Y2) then
			Middle = 1 
			Bottom = 3
			MiddleCompare = 3 
			BottomCompare = 2
		else 
			Middle = 3
			Bottom = 1
			MiddleCompare = 2
			BottomCompare = 3
		end
	end

	local gradients = makeGradients(triangle)
	local topToBottom = makeEdge(gradients,triangle, Top, Bottom)
	local topToMiddle = makeEdge(gradients,triangle, Top, Middle)
	local middleToBottom = makeEdge(gradients,triangle, Middle, Bottom)
	local middleIsLeft = true
	local pLeft,pRight

	if (BottomCompare > MiddleCompare) then
		middleIsLeft = false
		pLeft = topToBottom
		pRight = topToMiddle
	else
		middleIsLeft = true
		pLeft = topToMiddle
		pRight = topToBottom
	end

	local height = topToMiddle.height
 	
	--Special
	local halfPixelSize = pixelSize / 2
	
	while(height > 0) do
		height-=1
		drawScanLineForOccluder(gradients,pLeft,pRight, polygon, pixelSize, halfPixelSize)
		step(topToMiddle)
		step(topToBottom)
	end

	height = middleToBottom.height

	if (middleIsLeft)  then
		pLeft = middleToBottom
		pRight = topToBottom
	else 
		pLeft = topToBottom
		pRight = middleToBottom
	end

	while(height > 0) do
		height-=1
		drawScanLineForOccluder(gradients,pLeft,pRight, polygon, pixelSize, halfPixelSize)
		step(middleToBottom) 
		step(topToBottom)		
	end
	
	return false
end

return module

--[[

    Path: ServerScriptService → WeaponFrameworkServer
    Parent: WeaponFrameworkServer

        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
math.randomseed(tick())

local cs = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local rs = game:GetService("RunService")

local fw = game.ReplicatedStorage.WeaponFrameworkRep

local irPoints = Instance.new("Folder")
irPoints.Name = "InfraredPoints"
irPoints.Parent = workspace

local baseDot = Instance.new("Part")
baseDot.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball
baseDot.Size = Vector3.new(.9,.9,.9)
baseDot.Transparency = 1
baseDot.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Institutional white")
baseDot.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
baseDot.TopSurface = Enum.SurfaceType.Smooth
baseDot.BottomSurface = Enum.SurfaceType.Smooth
baseDot.CanCollide = false
baseDot.Massless = true

cs:AddTag(baseDot, "Untrackable")

local init = function()
	for _,model in pairs(game.ReplicatedStorage.WeaponFrameworkRep.Models:GetChildren()) do
		if model.PrimaryPart ~= nil then
			for _,v in pairs(model:GetDescendants()) do
				if v:IsA("BasePart") and v ~= model.PrimaryPart then
					local new = Instance.new("CFrameValue")
					new.Value = v.CFrame * model.PrimaryPart.CFrame:Inverse()
					new.Name = "CFOffset"
					new.Parent = v
				end
				
				if v:IsA("BasePart") then
					cs:AddTag(v, "Untrackable")
					v.CanCollide = false
				end
			end
		end
	end
end

function untagHumanoid(humanoid)
	if humanoid ~= nil then
		local tag = humanoid:findFirstChild("creator")
		if tag ~= nil then
			tag.Parent = nil
		end
	end
end

function tagHumanoid(humanoid, player)
	untagHumanoid(humanoid)
	local creator_tag = Instance.new("ObjectValue")
	creator_tag.Value = player
	creator_tag.Name = "creator"
	creator_tag.Parent = humanoid
end


local getHeliFromChild = function(v)
	heliFind = function(searchingIn)
		local functionality = searchingIn:FindFirstChild("Functionality")
		
		if functionality ~= nil then
			return functionality
		elseif searchingIn == workspace then
			return nil
		else
			return heliFind(searchingIn.Parent)
		end
	end
	
	local func = heliFind(v)
	
	if func ~= nil then
		func = func.Parent
	end
	
	return func
end

local getHumanoidFromChild = function(v)
	getHumanoid = function(v)
		local humanoid = v.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
		
		if humanoid ~= nil then
			return humanoid
		elseif v == workspace then
			return nil
		else
			return getHumanoid(v.Parent)
		end
	end
	
	local h = getHumanoid(v)
	
	return h
end

fw.Events.MarkLoopingSound.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(plr, sound, on)
	fw.Events.MarkLoopingSound:FireAllClients(plr, sound, on)
end)

fw.Events.ReplicateShot.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(plr, code, cf, muzzleVelocity, additionalVelocity, bulletType, ignoreTable, fxTable)
	if code ~= 19742 then

		plr:Kick("500 Internal Server Error")
	else
		fw.Events.ReplicateShot:FireAllClients(cf, muzzleVelocity, additionalVelocity, bulletType, ignoreTable, fxTable, plr)
	end
end)

end)

	else
		fw.Events.ReplicateFlare:FireAllClients(plr, cf, mV, iV, soundTable, true, heat)
	end
end)


fw.Events.Damage.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(plr, code, parts, bulletType, origin)
	if code ~= 19742 then
		plr:Kick("500 Internal Server Error")
	else
		local foundHelis = {}
		local foundHumanoids = {}
		
		for i,v in pairs(parts) do
			if v ~= "filler" then
				local dmg = (i == 1 and bulletType.DamageHumanoid.Value or bulletType.Explosive.ExplosiveDamageHumanoid.Value)
				local dmgV = (i == 1 and bulletType.DamageVehicle.Value or bulletType.Explosive.ExplosiveDamageVehicle.Value)
				
				local heli = getHeliFromChild(v)
				
				if heli ~= nil then
					local found = false
	
					
					for _,v in pairs(foundHelis) do
						if v[1] == heli then
							found = true
						end
					end
					
					if not found then
						table.insert(foundHelis, {heli, dmgV})
					end
				else
					local humanoid = getHumanoidFromChild(v)
					
					if humanoid ~= nil then
						local found = false
					
						for _,v in pairs(foundHumanoids) do
							if v[1] == humanoid then
								found = true
							end
						end
						
						local dmg = dmg
						
						if i ~= 1 then
							dmg = math.max((1 - (humanoid.Parent.Head.Position - origin).Magnitude / (bulletType.Explosive.ExplosiveRadius.Value)) * dmg, 0)
						end
						
						if not found then
							table.insert(foundHumanoids, {humanoid, dmg})
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
		
		for _,pair in pairs(foundHelis) do
			print(pair[2])
			pair[1].Functionality.Stats.Health.Value = pair[1].Functionality.Stats.Health.Value - (pair[2])
		end
		
		for _,pair in pairs(foundHumanoids) do
			tagHumanoid(pair[1])
			pair[1]:TakeDamage(pair[2])
		end
	end
end)

fw.Events.LaserDot.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(plr, code, action, tag, hit, offsetCF)
	if code ~= 19742 then
		plr:Kick("500 Internal Server Error")
	else
		if action == "new" then
			local new = baseDot:Clone()
			new.Name = tostring(tag)
			new.CFrame = hit.CFrame * offsetCF
			
			cs:AddTag(new, "Untrackable")
			cs:AddTag(new, "InfraredDot")
			
			local joint = Instance.new("Weld")
			joint.Name = "Hold"
			joint.Part0 = hit
			joint.Part1 = new
			joint.C0 = offsetCF
			joint.Parent = new
			
			new.Parent = irPoints
		elseif action == "update" then
			local dot = irPoints[tostring(tag)]
			
			if dot ~= nil then
				if dot:FindFirstChild("Hold") then
					dot.Hold.C0 = offsetCF
				else
					local joint = Instance.new("Weld")
					joint.Name = "Hold"
					joint.Part0 = hit
					joint.Part1 = dot
					joint.C0 = offsetCF
					joint.Parent = dot
				end
			end
		elseif action == "end" then
			pcall(function()
				local dot = irPoints[tostring(tag)]
				
				if dot ~= nil then
					dot:Destroy()
				end
			end)
		end
	end
end)

init()

while wait(1) do
	fw.LightingConditions.Ambient.Value = game.Lighting.Ambient
	fw.LightingConditions.OutdoorAmbient.Value = game.Lighting.OutdoorAmbient
	fw.LightingConditions.Brightness.Value = game.Lighting.Brightness
	fw.LightingConditions.GlobalShadows.Value = game.Lighting.GlobalShadows
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Modules/Boat.lua ---

--[[
    Boat (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Boat
-- Khizzer
-- October 9, 2023

local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local NetworkService: NetworkService;
local CooldownService;

type Boat = {
	Hull: Model;
	Body: Model;
	Config: Configuration;
};

local Boat = {}
Boat.__index = Boat

local function SetMassless(char, parts)
	if char then
		for i, v in next, char:GetDescendants() do
			if v:IsA('BasePart') then
				if not v.CustomPhysicalProperties then
					v.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(v.Material);
				end;
				parts[#parts + 1] = {v, v.CustomPhysicalProperties};
				local physicalProperties = v.CustomPhysicalProperties;
				v.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(
					0.01,
					physicalProperties.Friction,
					physicalProperties.Elasticity,
					physicalProperties.FrictionWeight,
					physicalProperties.ElasticityWeight
				);
			end;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, parts do
			if v[1] and v[2] and v[1]:IsDescendantOf(workspace) then
				v[1].CustomPhysicalProperties = v[2];
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


function Boat.new(boat: Boat, isEmergencyBoat: boolean)
	local self = setmetatable({}, Boat);

	self.Boat = boat;
	self.Body = boat.Body;
	self.Hull = boat.Hull;
	self.Platform = self.Hull.Platform;

	self.Config = boat.Config;

	self.IsEmergencyBoat = isEmergencyBoat;

	self:Weld();
	self:Unanchor();
	self:ConnectEvents();

	boat.Parent = workspace.Boats; --TODO: This needs to be done in boat spawner!!!
end;

function Boat:Weld()
	local platform = self.Platform;
	local platformCFrame = platform.CFrame;

	for _,v in next, self.Body:GetDescendants() do
		if v:GetAttribute('DoNotWeld') then continue; end;
		if v:IsA('BasePart') then
			local weld = Instance.new('Weld');
			weld.Part0 = v;
			weld.Part1 = platform;
			weld.C0 = v.CFrame:Inverse() * platformCFrame;
			weld.Parent = v;
			v.Massless = true;
		end;
	end;
end;

function Boat:Unanchor()
	for _,v in next, self.Hull:GetDescendants() do
		if v:IsA('BasePart') then
			v.Anchored = false;
		end;
	end;
	for _,v in next, self.Body:GetDescendants() do
		if v:IsA('BasePart') then
			v.Anchored = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

function Boat:ConnectEvents()
	local masslessCharParts = {};

	local boat = self.Boat;
	local platform = self.Platform;
	local body = self.Body;
	local config = self.Config;

	local isEmergencyBoat = self.IsEmergencyBoat;

	local sounds = platform.Sounds;
	local engine = sounds.Engine;
	local engineStart = sounds.EngineStart;
	local engineStop = sounds.EngineStop;

	local seat: VehicleSeat = self.Hull.VehicleSeat;

	local driver: Player?;
	local lastDriver: Player?;

	NetworkService.Connect('Boat', function(plr: Player, event: string, ...)
		if plr ~= driver then return; end;
		
		print(`Matched {plr.Name} to a boat`);

		if event == 'Engine' then
			if CooldownService:Check('BoatIgnition', plr) then return; end;
			CooldownService:Add('BoatIgnition', plr , 1.5);
			local enabled = boat:GetAttribute('Engine');
			if enabled then
				engineStop:Play();
				engineStart:Stop();
				engine:Stop();
				boat:SetAttribute('Engine', false);
			else
				engineStart:Play();
				engineStop:Stop();
				engine:Play();
				boat:SetAttribute('Engine', true);
			end;
		elseif event == 'NavigationLights' then
			local navigationLightsState = config.State:GetAttribute('NavigationLights');
			config.State:SetAttribute('NavigationLights', not navigationLightsState);
		elseif event == 'ELS' then
			local elsState = config.State:GetAttribute('ELS');
			config.State:SetAttribute('ELS', not elsState);
		elseif event == 'Anchor' then
			local state = ...;
			if state == true then
				sounds.Anchor:Play();
			end
			--TODO: Add anchor sounds
		elseif event == 'Siren' then
			local siren: Sound? = sounds:FindFirstChild('Siren');
			if siren then
				if siren.Playing then
					siren:Stop()
				else
					siren:Play();
				end;
			end
		end
	end)

	for _,v in next, body:GetChildren() do
		if not v:IsA('Seat') then continue; end;

		local seatMasslessCharParts = {};

		v:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Occupant'):Connect(function()
			local occupant = v.Occupant;
			if occupant then
				local char = occupant.Parent;
				SetMassless(char, seatMasslessCharParts);
			else
				SetMassless(nil, seatMasslessCharParts);
				seatMasslessCharParts = {};
			end;
		end);
	end;

	seat:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Occupant'):Connect(function()
		local occupant = seat.Occupant;

		if occupant then
			local char = occupant.Parent;
			SetMassless(char, masslessCharParts);
			driver = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(char);
			if not driver then return; end;

			if lastDriver and lastDriver ~= driver then
				-- TODO: setup the boat ownership objectvalue
			end;
			lastDriver = driver;
			self.LastDriver = driver;
			platform:SetNetworkOwner(driver);
			NetworkService.Send(driver, 'SetInventoryEnabled', false);
			NetworkService.Send(driver, 'Boat', 'Enter', boat, isEmergencyBoat);
			driver.DevEnableMouseLock = false;
		else
			if not driver then return; end; --safe to assume there is a driver if it changes to no occupant

			NetworkService.Send(driver, 'SetInventoryEnabled', true);
			NetworkService.Send(driver, 'Boat', 'Exit');
			SetMassless(nil, masslessCharParts);
			driver.DevEnableMouseLock = true;
			driver = nil;
		end
	end);
end;

function Boat:Start()
	CooldownService:Create('BoatIgnition')
end

function Boat:Init()
	CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService;
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end


return Boat
