--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Modules/Car.lua ---

--[[
    Car (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local NetworkService;

local wait;
local tick = tick;
local tonumber = tonumber;
local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;
local newInstance = Instance.new;
local newVector3 = Vector3.new;
local mathClamp = math.clamp;

local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService')
local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
local Players = game:GetService('Players')

local Functions;
local ProfileDataService;
local CooldownService;

local cooldownTag;

local GetPlayerFromCharacter;

local function GetSeatOccupant(seat)
    local seatWeld = seat:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld');
    if seatWeld then
        if seatWeld.Part1 then
            return seatWeld and seatWeld.Part1.Parent.Humanoid;
        end;
    end;
    return;
end;

local function SetMassless(char, parts)
	if char then
		for i, v in next, char:GetDescendants() do
			if v:IsA('BasePart') then
				if not v.CustomPhysicalProperties then
					v.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(v.Material);
				end;
				parts[#parts + 1] = {v, v.CustomPhysicalProperties};
				local physicalProperties = v.CustomPhysicalProperties;
				v.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(
					0.01,
					physicalProperties.Friction,
					physicalProperties.Elasticity,
					physicalProperties.FrictionWeight,
					physicalProperties.ElasticityWeight
				);
			end;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, parts do
			if v[1] and v[2] and v[1]:IsDescendantOf(workspace) then
				v[1].CustomPhysicalProperties = v[2];
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


local function Cooldown(duration, callback)
	local tag = tick();
	cooldownTag = tag;
	coroutineWrap(function()
		wait(duration);
		if cooldownTag == tag then
			callback();
		end;
	end)();
end;

local Car = {};
Car.__index = Car;

function Car.new(car, isEmergencyCar)
	local self = setmetatable({}, Car);

	--debug stage of game development only, remove when released

	if car.Parent ~= workspace.Cars then
		car.Parent = workspace.Cars;
		for _,v in next, workspace.Cars:GetChildren() do
			if v:IsA('Folder') then
				if not v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA('Model', true) then
					v:Destroy();
				end
			end
		end
	end;
	--if car.Parent ~= workspace.Cars then warn(car:GetFullName()..' is not a child of workspace.Cars!') end;

	local config = car.Config;
	local body = car.Body;
	local chassis = car.Chassis;
	local platform = chassis.Platform;
	local wheels = chassis.Wheels;

	self.Car = car;
	self.Config = config;
	self.Body = body;
	self.Chassis = chassis;
	self.Platform = platform;
	self.Wheels = wheels:GetChildren();
	self.IsEmergencyCar = isEmergencyCar;
	self.Health = config.State.Health
	self.Connections = {}
	self.CollideCooldown = false
	self.LadderInUse = false;
	self.Gas = self.Config.State.Gas;
	self.MaxGas = self.Gas:GetAttribute('MaxGas') or 100;

	if isEmergencyCar then
		self.ELS = config.ELS.Value;
		self.ELSPatterns = config.ELSPatterns;
	end;

	if car:GetAttribute('TrafficDirectors') then
		self.TDPatterns = config.TDPatterns;
	end

	local cf, size = body:GetBoundingBox();

	if body:FindFirstChild('CRASH_BOUNDS') then
		self.CRASH_BOUNDS = body:FindFirstChild('CRASH_BOUNDS')
	else
		self.CRASH_BOUNDS = Functions:Create 'Part' {
			Name = 'CRASH_BOUNDS';
			CanCollide = false;
			Size = size;
			Parent = body;
			Massless = true;
			Anchored = false;
			Transparency = 1;
			CFrame = cf;
		};
	end;

	CollectionService:AddTag(self.CRASH_BOUNDS, 'Ignore');
	CollectionService:AddTag(self.CRASH_BOUNDS, 'RayIgnore');

	self:Weld();
	self:SetupConstraints();
	self:Unanchor();
	self:SetupSounds();
	self:SetupLicensePlate();
	self:SetupGas();
	self:ConnectEvents();
end;

function Car:Weld()
	local platform = self.Platform;
	local platformCFrame = platform.CFrame;

	for i, v in next, self.Body:GetDescendants() do
		if v:IsA('BasePart') and (not v:FindFirstAncestor('Bed')) and (not v:FindFirstAncestor('Ladder')) and ((v.Parent.Name == "Antenna" and v.Name ~= "Wire") or v.Parent.Name ~= "Antenna") and (not v:GetAttribute('DontWeld', true)) then
			local weld = newInstance('Weld');
			weld.Part0 = v;
			weld.Part1 = platform;
			weld.C0 = v.CFrame:Inverse() * platformCFrame;
			weld.Parent = v;
		end;
		if v:IsA('Seat') or v:IsA('VehicleSeat') then
			v.Transparency = 1;
		end;
	end;

	for i, v in next, self.Wheels do
		local wheel = v.Wheel;
		local wheelModel = wheel.WheelModel;
		local primaryPart = wheelModel.PrimaryPart;
		local primaryPartCFrame = primaryPart.CFrame;

		for i2, v2 in next, wheelModel:GetDescendants() do
			if v2:IsA('BasePart') and v2 ~= primaryPart then
				local weld = newInstance('Weld');
				weld.Part0 = v2;
				weld.Part1 = primaryPart;
				weld.C0 = v2.CFrame:Inverse() * primaryPartCFrame;
				weld.Parent = v2;
			end;
		end;

		local weld = newInstance('Weld');
		weld.Part0 = primaryPart;
		weld.Part1 = wheel;
		weld.C0 = primaryPartCFrame:Inverse() * wheel.CFrame;
		weld.Parent = primaryPart;
	end;
end;

function Car:SetupConstraints()
	local platform = self.Platform;
	local platformCFrame = platform.CFrame;

	local ATTACHMENT_Y_OFFSET = -(platform.Size.Y * 0.5);
	local ATTACHMENT_ORIENTATION = newVector3(0, 0, -90);

	local wheelAttachments = {};

	for i, v in next, self.Wheels do
		local suffix = v.Name:gsub('Wheel', '');

		local wheel = v.Wheel;

		do
			local physicalProperties = wheel.CustomPhysicalProperties;

			local defaultFriction = newInstance('NumberValue');
			defaultFriction.Name = 'DefaultFriction';
			defaultFriction.Value = physicalProperties.Friction;
			defaultFriction.Parent = wheel;

			local defaultFrictionWeight = newInstance('NumberValue');
			defaultFrictionWeight.Name = 'DefaultFrictionWeight';
			defaultFrictionWeight.Value = physicalProperties.FrictionWeight;
			defaultFrictionWeight.Parent = wheel;

			local health = newInstance('IntValue');
			health.Name = 'Health';
			health.Value = 100;
			health.Parent = wheel;
		end;

		do
			if not platform:FindFirstChild('Attachment' .. suffix) then
			local attachment1 = wheel.Attachment1;
			local attachment0Pos = platformCFrame:PointToObjectSpace(attachment1.WorldPosition);
			local attachment0 = newInstance('Attachment');
			attachment0.Name = 'Attachment' .. suffix;
			attachment0.Parent = platform;
			attachment0.Position = newVector3(attachment0Pos.X, ATTACHMENT_Y_OFFSET, attachment0Pos.Z);
			attachment0.Orientation = ATTACHMENT_ORIENTATION;
			end;

			local attachment1 = wheel.Attachment1;
			local attachment0 = platform:FindFirstChild('Attachment' .. suffix)

			wheelAttachments[suffix] = {attachment0, attachment1};
		end;

		do
			local tire = wheel.WheelModel.PrimaryPart;
			local tirePosition = tire.Position;

			local tread = newInstance('Part');
			tread.Name = 'Tread';
			tread.Anchored = true;
			tread.CanCollide = false;
			tread.Massless = true;
			tread.Size = tire.Size;
			tread.CFrame = CFrame.new(tirePosition, tirePosition + tire.CFrame.LookVector);
			tread.Transparency = 1;
			tread.Parent = wheel;

			local weld = newInstance('Weld');
			weld.Part0 = tread;
			weld.Part1 = platform;
			weld.C0 = tread.CFrame:Inverse() * platformCFrame;
			weld.Parent = tread;

			local attachment0 = newInstance('Attachment');
			attachment0.Name = 'Attachment0';
			attachment0.Position = newVector3(tire.Size.Y * 0.5, 0, 0);
			attachment0.Parent = tread;

			local attachment1 = attachment0:Clone();
			attachment1.Name = 'Attachment1';
			attachment1.Position = newVector3(-tire.Size.Y * 0.5, 0, 0);
			attachment1.Parent = tread;

			local trail = newInstance('Trail');
			trail.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new());
			trail.Lifetime = 10;
			trail.LightInfluence = 0.9;
			trail.Enabled = false;
			trail.Attachment0 = attachment0;
			trail.Attachment1 = attachment1;
			trail.MaxLength = 80;
			trail.Parent = tread;

			local smoke = newInstance('Smoke');
			smoke.Size = 0.1;
			smoke.Opacity = 0.4;
			smoke.Enabled = false;
			smoke.Parent = tread;
		end;
	end;

	for i, v in next, platform:GetChildren() do
		if v:IsA('CylindricalConstraint') then
			local suffix = v.Name:gsub('Cylindrical', '');

			local attachments = wheelAttachments[suffix];
			v.Attachment0 = attachments[1];
			v.Attachment1 = attachments[2];
		elseif v:IsA('SpringConstraint') then
			local suffix = v.Name:gsub('Spring', '');

			local attachments = wheelAttachments[suffix];
			v.Attachment0 = attachments[1];
			v.Attachment1 = attachments[2];
		end;
	end;
end;

function Car:Unanchor()
	for i, v in next, self.Car:GetDescendants() do
		if v:IsA('BasePart') then
			v.Anchored = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

function Car:Anchor()
	if self.Body then
		for i, v in next, self.Car:GetDescendants() do
			if v:IsA('BasePart') then
				if self.Body.Ladder then
					if not v:IsDescendantOf(self.Body.Ladder) then
						v.Anchored = true;
					end
				else
					v.Anchored = true;
				end
			end;
		end;
	end
end;

function Car:SetupSounds()
	local backgroundSound = newInstance('Sound');
	backgroundSound.Name = 'Background';
	backgroundSound.SoundId = 'rbxassetid://9172423309';
	backgroundSound.Volume = 0;
	backgroundSound.Looped = true;
	backgroundSound.Parent = self.Platform.Sounds;

	backgroundSound:Play();

	local radioSound = Functions:Create('Sound'){
		Name = 'Radio';
		Volume = 0.5;
		Looped = true;
		Parent = self.Platform.Sounds;
		MaxDistance = 75;
	};

	local muffle = Functions:Create('EqualizerSoundEffect'){
		Name = 'Muffle';
		HighGain = -30;
		MidGain = -30;
		LowGain = 0;
		Enabled = true;
		Parent = radioSound;
	};
end;

function Car:SetupLicensePlate()
	for _,v in next, self.Body:GetChildren() do
		if v.Name == 'LicensePlate' then
			local licensePlate = self.Config.LicensePlate;
			local licensePlateLabel = v.LicensePlateGUI.LicensePlateLabel;

			licensePlateLabel.Text = licensePlate.Value;

			licensePlate.Changed:Connect(function()
				licensePlateLabel.Text = licensePlate.Value;
			end);
		end
	end
end;

function Car:SetupGas()
	local seat = self.Chassis.VehicleSeat;
	local gas = self.Gas;
	local car = self.Car;

	local function SaveGasData()
		local ownerPlr = Players:FindFirstChild(car:GetAttribute('Owner'));
		local occupant = GetSeatOccupant(seat);
		if occupant and ownerPlr then
			local occupantPlr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(occupant.Parent);
			if ownerPlr == occupantPlr then
				local carData = ProfileDataService.GetData(ownerPlr, 'BoughtCars');
				for _,v in next, carData do
					if tonumber(v.ID) == car.Config.ID.Value then
						if v.Gas == nil then v.Gas = 100; end;
						v.Gas = gas.Value;
					end;
				end;
				ProfileDataService.SetData(ownerPlr, 'BoughtCars', carData);
			end;
		end
	end;

	coroutineWrap(function()
		while true do
			if gas.Value > 0 and self.Car:GetAttribute('Engine') then
				gas.Value = mathClamp(gas.Value - 6, 0, self.MaxGas);
				SaveGasData();
			end;
			task.wait(150);
		end;
	end)();
end;

function Car:ConnectEvents()
	local car = self.Car;
	local config = self.Config;
	local state = config.State;
	local body = self.Body;
	local platform = self.Platform;
	local seat: VehicleSeat = self.Chassis.VehicleSeat;
	local ladderseat = nil;
	local laddermodel;
	local ladderv;
	local ladderh;
	local l1weld;
	local l2weld;
	local l3weld;
	local ladder1out = false;
	local ladder2out = false;
	local ladder3out = false;
	local ladder3tweened = false;
	local ladder2tweened = false;
	if self.Body:FindFirstChild("Ladder") then
		if self.Body:FindFirstChild("Ladder"):FindFirstChild("Seat") then
			ladderseat = self.Body.Ladder.Seat;
		end
	end
	if ladderseat ~= nil then
		laddermodel = self.Body.Ladder
		ladderv = laddermodel.VMotor
		ladderh = laddermodel.HMotor
		l1weld = laddermodel.Ladder["L1"]
		l2weld = laddermodel.Ladder["L2"]
		l3weld = laddermodel.Ladder["L3"]
	end
	local laddertweens = {};

	local sounds = self.Platform.Sounds;
	local engineStart = sounds.EngineStart;
	local engine = sounds.Engine;
	local engineStop = sounds.EngineStop;
	local horn = sounds.Horn;

	local reverselights = state.Reverselights;
	local indicators = state.Indicators;
	local hazards = state.Hazards;

	local ELSPatterns = self.ELSPatterns;
	local currentPattern = ELSPatterns and ELSPatterns.CurrentPattern;
	local sirens = platform:FindFirstChild('Sirens');
	local TDPatterns = self.TDPatterns;
	local currentTDPattern = TDPatterns and TDPatterns.CurrentPattern;

	local isEmergencyCar = self.IsEmergencyCar;

	local driver;
	local ladderDriver;
	local lastDriver;
	local masslessCharParts;

	NetworkService.Connect('Car', function(plr: Player, event: string, ...)
		if event == 'Ladder' then
			if plr ~= ladderDriver then
				return;
			end;
		else
			if plr ~= driver then
				return;
			end;
		end;
		if event:sub(1, 3) == 'ELS' then
			local pattern = tonumber(event:sub(4, 4));

			if pattern ~= 0 then
				local patternModule = ELSPatterns['Pattern' .. pattern];

				local enabled = currentPattern.Value == patternModule;

				if enabled then
					currentPattern.Value = nil;
					return;
				end;

				currentPattern.Value = patternModule;
			else
				currentPattern.Value = nil;
			end;
		elseif event:sub(1,2) == 'TD' then
			local pattern = event:sub(3);
			if pattern ~= 0 then
				local patternModule = TDPatterns[pattern];

				local enabled = currentTDPattern.Value == patternModule;

				if enabled then
					currentTDPattern.Value = nil;
					return;
				end;

				currentTDPattern.Value = patternModule;
			else
				currentTDPattern.Value = nil;
			end
		elseif event == 'Engine' then
			if CooldownService:Check('EngineIgnition', plr) then return; end;
			CooldownService:Add('EngineIgnition', plr , 1.5);
			local enabled = car:GetAttribute('Engine');
			if enabled then
				engineStop:Play();
				engineStart:Stop();
				engine:Stop();
				car:SetAttribute('Engine', false);
			else
				engineStart:Play();
				engineStop:Stop();
				engine:Play();
				car:SetAttribute('Engine', true);
			end;
		elseif event:sub(1, 5) == 'Siren' then
			local sirenTable = HttpService:JSONDecode(event:sub(6, #event));
			--Format: ^ {'Wail', 'Prty'} etc...

			if #sirenTable ~= 0 then
				--Stop sirens not in the sirenTable
				for i, v in next, sirens:GetChildren() do
					if not table.find(sirenTable, v.Name) then
						v:Stop();
					end;
				end;
				--Enable each siren
				for _,siren in next, sirenTable do
					local sound = sirens[siren]; --The actual sound object

					local enabled = sound.IsPlaying;

					if not enabled then
						sound:Play();
					end;
				end
			else
				for i, v in next, sirens:GetChildren() do
					v:Stop();
				end;
			end;
		elseif event == 'Headlights' then
			local headlights = config.State.Headlights;
			headlights.Value = not headlights.Value;
		elseif event == 'Reverselights' then
			reverselights.Value = ...;
		elseif event == 'LeftIndicators' then
			hazards.Value = false;
			indicators.Value = (indicators.Value == -1) and 0 or -1;
		elseif event == 'RightIndicators' then
			hazards.Value = false;
			indicators.Value = (indicators.Value == 1) and 0 or 1;
		elseif event == 'Hazards' then
			indicators.Value = 0;
			hazards.Value = not hazards.Value;

		elseif event == 'Honk' then
			local Args = {...}
			if Args[1] == true then
				horn:Stop()
				horn:Play()
			else
				horn:Stop()
			end
		elseif event == 'Lock' then
			if plr.Name ~= self.Car:GetAttribute('Owner') then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'You cannot lock someone else\'s car.'); end;
			local locked = config.State.Locked;
			locked.Value = not locked.Value;
		elseif event == 'SpotlightDirection' then
			local movementValue = config.State.Spotlight.Movement;
			local direction = ...;
			movementValue.Value = direction;
		elseif event == 'SpotlightToggle' then
			local toggle = config.State.Spotlight.Toggle;
			toggle.Value = not toggle.Value;
		elseif event == 'ParkingBrake' then
			local newStatus = ...;
			local sounds = car.Chassis.Platform.Sounds;

			local parkingBrakeSound = if newStatus == true then sounds.ParkingBrakeOn else sounds.ParkingBrakeOff;
			parkingBrakeSound:Play();
		elseif event == 'Ladder' then
			local args = {...}
			if args[1] == "Left" then
				self:Anchor()
				self.LadderInUse = true
				if args[2] == true then
					if ladderh then
						ladderh.DesiredAngle = 1.6
						ladderh.MaxVelocity = 0.002
					end
				else
					if ladderh then
						ladderh.DesiredAngle = 1.6
						ladderh.MaxVelocity = 0
					end
				end
			elseif args[1] == "Right" then
				self:Anchor()
				self.LadderInUse = true
				if args[2] == true then
					if ladderh then
						ladderh.DesiredAngle = -1.6
						ladderh.MaxVelocity = 0.002
					end
				else
					if ladderh then
						ladderh.DesiredAngle = -1.6
						ladderh.MaxVelocity = 0
					end
				end
			elseif args[1] == "Up" then
				self:Anchor()
				self.LadderInUse = true
				if args[2] == true then
					if ladderv then
						ladderv.DesiredAngle = 0.7
						ladderv.MaxVelocity = 0.002
					end
				else
					if ladderv then
						ladderv.DesiredAngle = 0.7
						ladderv.MaxVelocity = 0
					end
				end
			elseif args[1] == "Down" then
				self:Anchor()
				self.LadderInUse = true
				if args[2] == true then
					if ladderv then
						ladderv.DesiredAngle = 0
						ladderv.MaxVelocity = 0.002
					end
				else
					if ladderv then
						ladderv.DesiredAngle = 0
						ladderv.MaxVelocity = 0
					end
				end
			elseif args[1] == "Reset" then
				self:Unanchor()
				self.LadderInUse = false
				if ladderv and ladderh then
					ladderv.DesiredAngle = 0
					ladderv.MaxVelocity = 0.002
					ladderh.DesiredAngle = 0
					ladderh.MaxVelocity = 0.002
					for i,t in pairs(laddertweens) do
						if type(t) == "userdata" and t then
							t:Cancel()
							t:Destroy()
						end
					end
					if l2weld.L2Weld.Weld.C0.X < 0 then
						local Tween = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(l2weld.L2Weld.Weld, TweenInfo.new(4, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, false, 0), {C0 = CFrame.new(0,0,0)})
						table.insert(laddertweens, (#laddertweens + 1), Tween)
						Tween:Play()
						Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
							Tween:Destroy()
						end)
					end
					if l3weld.L3Weld.Weld.C0.X < 0 then
						local Tween = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(l3weld.L3Weld.Weld, TweenInfo.new(4, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, false, 0), {C0 = CFrame.new(0,0,0)})
						table.insert(laddertweens, (#laddertweens + 1), Tween)
						Tween:Play()
						Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
							Tween:Destroy()
						end)
					end
				end
			elseif args[1] == "Out" then
				self:Anchor()
				self.LadderInUse = true
				if args[2] == true then
					if l2weld.L2Weld.Weld.C0.X > -17 then
						local Tween = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(l2weld.L2Weld.Weld, TweenInfo.new(4, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, false, 0), {C0 = CFrame.new(-25,0,0)})
						table.insert(laddertweens, (#laddertweens + 1), Tween)
						Tween:Play()
						Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
							Tween:Destroy()
						end)
					elseif l3weld.L3Weld.Weld.C0.X > -35 then
						local Tween = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(l3weld.L3Weld.Weld, TweenInfo.new(4, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, false, 0), {C0 = CFrame.new(-33,0,0)})
						table.insert(laddertweens, (#laddertweens + 1), Tween)
						Tween:Play()
						Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
							Tween:Destroy()
						end)
					end
				else
					for i,t in pairs(laddertweens) do
						if type(t) == "userdata" and t then
							t:Cancel()
							t:Destroy()
						end
					end
				end
			elseif args[1] == "In" then
				self.LadderInUse = true
				self:Anchor()
				if args[2] == true then
					if l2weld.L2Weld.Weld.C0.X < 0 then
						local Tween = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(l2weld.L2Weld.Weld, TweenInfo.new(4, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, false, 0), {C0 = CFrame.new(0,0,0)})
						table.insert(laddertweens, (#laddertweens + 1), Tween)
						Tween:Play()
						Tween.Completed:Once(function()
							Tween:Destroy()
						end)
					elseif l3weld.L3Weld.Weld.C0.X < 0 then
						local Tween = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(l3weld.L3Weld.Weld, TweenInfo.new(4, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, false, 0), {C0 = CFrame.new(0,0,0)})
						table.insert(laddertweens, (#laddertweens + 1), Tween)
						Tween:Play()
						Tween.Completed:Once(function()
							Tween:Destroy()
						end)
					end
				else
					for i,t in pairs(laddertweens) do
						if type(t) == "userdata" and t then
							t:Cancel()
							t:Destroy()
						end
					end
				end
			end;
		end
	end);

	--[[

	self.Connections['collision'] = self.CRASH_BOUNDS.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
		if _G.CarDamages == nil then
			_G.CarDamages = {}
		end
		if driver then
			if _G.CarDamages[driver.UserId] == nil then
				_G.CarDamages[driver.UserId] = {}
			end
		end
		if self.CollideCooldown == true then return; end
		if hit and hit.Parent and hit:IsA('BasePart') and not hit.Parent:IsA('Accessory') and not hit:IsDescendantOf(self.Car) and not hit.Parent:FindFirstChild('Torso') and hit.CanCollide == true then --and not hit.Transparency == 1 then
			local hitMass = Functions:GetMass(hit);
			if hit.Transparency == 1 then return; end;
			if hit.Position.Y < (self.CRASH_BOUNDS.Position.Y/2) then return; end
			if hitMass > 0 then
				task.spawn(function()
					self.CollideCooldown = true
					task.wait(0.5)
					self.CollideCooldown = false
				end)
				local speed = self.CRASH_BOUNDS.Velocity.Magnitude;
				if speed >= 30 and speed < 50 then
					print('Crashed into part at speed:' , speed, ' with mass', hitMass)
					self.Health.Value -= 5;
					if driver then
						_G.CarDamages[driver.UserId][self.Config.SpawnerSettings.ID.Value] = self.Health.Value
					end
				elseif speed >= 50 and speed < 80 then
					self.Health.Value -= 10;
					if driver then
						_G.CarDamages[driver.UserId][self.Config.SpawnerSettings.ID.Value] = self.Health.Value
					end
				elseif speed > 80 then
					self.Health.Value -= 15;
					if driver then
						_G.CarDamages[driver.UserId][self.Config.SpawnerSettings.ID.Value] = self.Health.Value
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end)

	]]

	self.Health.Changed:Connect(function(newValue)
		if newValue <= 0 then
			if _G.CarDamages == nil then
				_G.CarDamages = {}
			end
			if driver then
				if _G.CarDamages[driver.UserId] == nil then
					_G.CarDamages[driver.UserId] = {}
				end
			end
			if driver then
				_G.CarDamages[driver.UserId][self.Config.ID.Value] = 0
			end
			local smoke = game.ServerStorage.SmokeParticle:Clone();
			smoke.Parent = self.CRASH_BOUNDS;
			if seat.Occupant then
				seat.Occupant.Parent.Humanoid.Jump = true;
				task.wait(0.25)
				CollectionService:RemoveTag(seat, 'VehicleSeat')
				local _config = self.Config;
				local _state = _config.State;
				_state.Hazards.Value = true;
			end
			if ladderseat then
				if ladderseat.Occupant then
					ladderseat.Occupant.Parent.Humanoid.Jump = true;
					task.wait(0.25)
					CollectionService:RemoveTag(ladderseat, 'Seat')
				end
			end
		elseif newValue == 100 then
			local smoke = self.CRASH_BOUNDS:FindFirstChild('SmokeParticle');
			if not smoke then return; end;
			smoke:Destroy();
			CollectionService:AddTag(seat, 'VehicleSeat');
			CollectionService:AddTag(ladderseat, 'Seat')
		end
	end)

	for i, v in next, body:GetChildren() do
		if v:IsA('Seat') or v:IsA('VehicleSeat') then
			--local lastOccupant;
			local seatMasslessCharParts;

			v:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Occupant'):Connect(function()
				local occupant = v.Occupant;
				if occupant then
					local char = occupant.Parent;
					if not v:GetAttribute('LastOccupant') then
						v:SetAttribute('LastOccupant', char.Name);
						NetworkService.Send(game.Players[char.Name], 'RADIO_MUFFLE', body.Parent, false);
					end;
					seatMasslessCharParts = {};
					SetMassless(char, seatMasslessCharParts);
					--lastOccupant = char;
				else
					local lastOccupant = v:GetAttribute('LastOccupant');
					if game.Players:FindFirstChild(lastOccupant) then
						NetworkService.Send(game.Players[lastOccupant], 'RADIO_MUFFLE', body.Parent, true);
						v:SetAttribute('LastOccupant', nil);
					end
					SetMassless(nil, seatMasslessCharParts);
					seatMasslessCharParts = {};
					--lastOccupant = nil;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;


	seat:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Occupant'):Connect(function()
		local occupant = seat.Occupant;

		if occupant then
			if self.LadderInUse then
				if game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayerFromCharacter(occupant.Parent) ~= nil then
					NetworkService.Send(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayerFromCharacter(occupant.Parent), 'Car', 'Exit');
				end
			else
				local char = occupant.Parent;

				masslessCharParts = {};
				SetMassless(char, masslessCharParts);

				driver = GetPlayerFromCharacter(char);
				if driver.Team.Name == 'Civilian' then
					if config.State.Locked.Value == true and driver.Name ~= self.Car:GetAttribute('Owner') then
						seat.SeatWeld:Destroy();
						return;
					end;
				end;
				if lastDriver and lastDriver ~= driver then
					local lastDriverCar = lastDriver.Car;
					if lastDriverCar.Value == car then
						lastDriverCar.Value = nil;
					end;
				end;
				lastDriver = driver;
				self.LastDriver = driver;
				car:SetAttribute('LastDriver', driver.Name)
				driver.Car.Value = car;
				if not seat:GetAttribute('LastOccupant') then
					seat:SetAttribute('LastOccupant', char.Name);
					NetworkService.Send(game.Players[char.Name], 'RADIO_MUFFLE', body.Parent, false);
				end;
				platform:SetNetworkOwner(driver);
				NetworkService.Send(driver, 'SetInventoryEnabled', false);
				NetworkService.Send(driver, 'Car', 'Enter', car, isEmergencyCar);
				driver.DevEnableMouseLock = false;
			end
		elseif driver then
			horn:Stop();
			NetworkService.Send(driver, 'Car', 'Exit');
			driver.DevEnableMouseLock = true;
			self.Connections['collision'] = nil;

			SetMassless(nil, masslessCharParts);
			masslessCharParts = {};

			driver = nil;
			local lastOccupant = seat:GetAttribute('LastOccupant');
			if game.Players:FindFirstChild(lastOccupant) then
				NetworkService.Send(game.Players[lastOccupant], 'RADIO_MUFFLE', body.Parent, true);
				seat:SetAttribute('LastOccupant', nil);
			end

			reverselights.Value = false;
			if sirens then
				for i, v in next, sirens:GetChildren() do
					v:Stop();
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end);

	if ladderseat then
		ladderseat:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Occupant'):Connect(function()
			local occupant = ladderseat.Occupant;

			if occupant then
				local char = occupant.Parent;

				masslessCharParts = {};
				SetMassless(char, masslessCharParts);
				local plr  = GetPlayerFromCharacter(char)
				if plr  ~= nil then
					if plr.Team.Name == 'Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service' then
						ladderDriver = plr;
						NetworkService.Send(ladderDriver, 'Ladder', 'Enter', car, isEmergencyCar);
						NetworkService.Send(ladderDriver, 'OpenLadder', true);
					else
						char:WaitForChild("Humanoid").Jump = true
					end
				end
			elseif ladderDriver then
				NetworkService.Send(ladderDriver, 'Ladder', 'Exit');
				NetworkService.Send(ladderDriver, 'OpenLadder', false);
				self.Connections['collision'] = nil;

				SetMassless(nil, masslessCharParts);
				masslessCharParts = {};
			end;
		end);
	end;
end;

function Car:Start()
	CooldownService:Create('EngineIgnition');
end;

function Car:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	wait = self.Shared.Wait;
	GetPlayerFromCharacter = self.Shared.GetPlayerFromCharacter;
	Functions = self.Modules.Functions;
	ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
	CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService
end;

return Car;

--[[
    Building (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules → Classes

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local ClassInit = require(ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.ClassInit);

local Building = ClassInit();

function Building:Constructor(model: Model)
    self.Model = model;
    self.WhitelistedUsers = {};
end;

function Building:SetOwner(userID: number)
    self.Owner = userID;
    self.WhitelistedUsers[userID] = true;
    self.OwnerUsername = Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(userID);
    self.OwnerInstance = Players:FindFirstChild(self.OwnerUsername);
    self.Breached = false;

    local ownerDisplay = self.Model:FindFirstChild('OwnerDisplay');
    if not ownerDisplay then
        warn('No owner display found');
        return;
    else
        local ownerLabel = ownerDisplay:FindFirstChild('OwnerLabel', true);
        ownerLabel.Text = 'Owner: '..self.OwnerUsername;
    end;
end;

function Building:SetVacant()
    self.Owner = nil;
    self.WhitelistedUsers = {};
    self.OwnerUsername = nil;
    self.OwnerInstance = nil;

    local ownerDisplay = self.Model:FindFirstChild('OwnerDisplay');
    if not ownerDisplay then 
        warn('No owner display found');
        return;
    else
        local ownerLabel = ownerDisplay:FindFirstChild('OwnerLabel', true);
        ownerLabel.Text = 'Vacant';
    end;
end;

function Building:AddWhitelistedUser(userID: number)
    self.WhitelistedUsers[userID] = true;
end;

function Building:RemoveWhitelistedUser(userID: number)
    self.WhitelistedUsers[userID] = nil;
end;

return Building

--[[
    Warehouse (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules → Classes
    Parent: Classes
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53

-- Warehouse
-- Khizzer
-- June 17, 2022



local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local ClassInit = require(ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.ClassInit);

local BaseClass = require(script.Parent.Building);

local Warehouse = ClassInit()
Warehouse:Extends(BaseClass);

function Warehouse:Constructor(model, optionalData)
    self.ExteriorModel = model;

    self.Supplies = 0;
    self.MaxSupplies = 100;

    self.Money = 0;
    self.MaxMoney = 100000;

    self.InfoPart = model:FindFirstChild('InfoPart');

    if optionalData then
        for i,v in optionalData do
            self[i] = v;
        end;
    end;

    local fakeInterior = model:Clone();
    fakeInterior.Name = "WarehouseInterior";
    fakeInterior.Parent = workspace;
    fakeInterior.InfoPart:Destroy();
    --pivot it to somewhere under the map
    fakeInterior:PivotTo(CFrame.new(Vector3.new(math.random(0, 10000), 9999, math.random(0, 10000))) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0));
    self.InteriorModel = fakeInterior;

    self.Teleports = {
        Inside = self.InteriorModel.Teleports.Inside;
        Outside = self.ExteriorModel.Teleports.Outside;
    };


    CollectionService:AddTag(self.Teleports.Inside, "WarehouseLeave");
end;

function Warehouse:AddSupplies(amount)
    self.Supplies += amount;
    self.Supplies = math.clamp(self.Supplies, 0, self.MaxSupplies);
end;

function Warehouse:AddMoney(amount)
    self.Money += amount;
    self.Money = math.clamp(self.Money, 0, self.MaxMoney);
end;

function Warehouse:SubtractSupplies(amount)
    self.Supplies -= amount;
    self.Supplies = math.clamp(self.Supplies, 0, self.MaxSupplies);
end;

function Warehouse:SubtractMoney(amount)
    self.Money -= amount;
    self.Money = math.clamp(self.Money, 0, self.MaxMoney);
end;

return Warehouse

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Modules/DamageCharacter.lua ---

--[[
    DamageCharacter (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Damage Character
-- Khizzer
-- March 24, 2022

local Players = game:GetService('Players');

return function(character, damage, killer)
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid');
    if not humanoid then return; end;
    local plr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(character);
    if not plr then return; end;
    if plr:GetAttribute('Ragdoll') == true then return; end;

    if damage ~= damage then return; end;
    damage = math.abs(damage);


    if humanoid.Health - damage > 1 then
        humanoid.Health -= damage;
    else
        plr:SetAttribute('Ragdoll', true);
        humanoid.Health = 1;

        if killer then
            plr:SetAttribute('Killer', killer.Name);
            _G.Aero.Services.LogsService:AddLog('Kills', `{killer.Name} killed {plr.Name}`);
        end
    end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Modules/DataService.lua ---

--[[
    DataService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local DataModule = {};

local players = game:GetService('Players');
local datastore = game:GetService('DataStoreService'):GetDataStore('vancouvercityv2db_9');

local type = type;
local tostring = tostring;
local GetAsync = datastore.GetAsync;
local SetAsync = datastore.SetAsync;
local RemoveAsync = datastore.RemoveAsync;
local GetUserIdFromNameAsync = players.GetUserIdFromNameAsync;

function DataModule.Get(plr, data)
    if type(plr) == 'string' then
        return GetAsync(datastore, tostring(GetUserIdFromNameAsync(players, plr)) .. data);
    elseif type(plr) == 'number' then
        return GetAsync(datastore, tostring(plr) .. data);
    end;

    return GetAsync(datastore, tostring(plr.UserId) .. data);
end;

function DataModule.Set(plr, data, value)
    if type(plr) == 'string' then
        SetAsync(datastore, tostring(GetUserIdFromNameAsync(players, plr)) .. data, value);
    end;

    SetAsync(datastore, tostring(plr.UserId) .. data, value);
end;

function DataModule.Remove(plr, data)
    if type(plr) == 'string' then
        RemoveAsync(datastore, tostring(GetUserIdFromNameAsync(players, plr)) .. data);
    end;

    RemoveAsync(datastore, tostring(plr.UserId) .. data);
end;

return DataModule;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Modules/ElectionDataService.lua ---

--[[
    ElectionDataService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
-- Election Data Service
-- Khizzer
-- October 16, 2021



local ElectionDataService = {}

local GlobalStorage = require(script.Parent.GlobalStorage);

local electionStore = GlobalStorage.new(if RunService:IsStudio() then "ElectionTest" else "ElectionData");

local Get = electionStore.Get;
local Update = electionStore.Update;
local NotificationService;

local function ReturnFormattedTime(ostime : number)
    local dt = DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(ostime);
    return dt:FormatUniversalTime('LLL', 'en-US');
end

function ElectionDataService.InitialiseElection(electionID: string, title: string, candidates: {string}, endTime: number, winners: number)
    local electionDetails = ReplicatedStorage.ElectionDetails;

    local dataTable = {
        Title = title,
        Candidates = {},
        AlreadyVoted = {},
        SuspVoters = {},
        EndTime = os.time() + endTime,
        Winners = winners or 1
    };

    for _,v in next, candidates do
        dataTable['Candidates'][v] = 0;
    end;

    dataTable['Candidates']['Spoil my ballot'] = 0;

    for key,val in dataTable do
        --SetAsync(datastore, electionID..key, val);
        Update(electionStore, electionID..key, function(oldKey)
            return val;
        end);
    end;

    Update(electionStore, 'CurrentElection', function(oldKey)
        return electionID;
    end);

    electionDetails:SetAttribute('GUID', electionID);
    electionDetails:SetAttribute('Title', dataTable.Title);
    electionDetails:SetAttribute('EndTime', dataTable.EndTime);
    electionDetails:SetAttribute('Winners', dataTable.Winners);

    NotificationService.SendAll('Election', 'A new election has been created! End time: '..ReturnFormattedTime(dataTable.EndTime) .. '. There are '..tostring(winners or 1)..' possible winners.', nil, 'Purple');
end;

function ElectionDataService.GetCurrentRunningElection()
    return Get(electionStore, 'CurrentElection');
end;

function ElectionDataService.GetWinners(electionID: string)
    local endTime = ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'EndTime');
    local candidates = ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'Candidates');
    -- local winners = ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'Winners');

    local sortedCandidates = {};
    local resultsTable = {};

    if endTime then
        if os.time() > endTime then
            local voters = 0
            for _ in ElectionDataService.Get(electionID, 'AlreadyVoted') or {} do
                voters += 1
            end

            local spoiledBallots = 0;
            for candidate in candidates do
                table.insert(sortedCandidates, candidate);
            end;
            table.sort(sortedCandidates, function(a,b)
                return candidates[a] > candidates[b];
            end);

            for _, candidateName in sortedCandidates do
                local votes = candidates[candidateName]
                if candidateName == "Spoil my ballot" or candidateName == "SPOIL_MY_BALLOT" then
                    spoiledBallots += votes;
                    continue;
                end
                -- local isWinner = _ <= winners;
                table.insert(resultsTable, `{candidateName}: {votes} vote{if votes == 1 then '' else 's'}`);
            end;

            table.insert(resultsTable, `Spoiled ballots: {spoiledBallots}`);
            table.insert(resultsTable, `Total ballots: {voters}`);

            return resultsTable;
        else
            return "Election is in progress.";
        end;
    else
        return "No election found.";
    end;
end;

function ElectionDataService.Get(electionID: string, dataType: string)
    return Get(electionStore, electionID..dataType);
end;

function ElectionDataService.Update(electionID, dataType, transform)
    Update(electionStore, electionID..dataType, transform);
end;

function tabletostring(tbl,mode,space)
    local stringResult = (space and " {") or "{"
    local mode = mode or 1
    local space = space or 0
    if type(tbl) == "table" then
        local amount = 0
        for Index, Value in pairs(tbl) do
            local tablesize = 0
            if type(tbl) == "table" then
                for _,_ in pairs(tbl) do tablesize=tablesize+1 end
            end
            amount=amount+1
            if mode==2 then stringResult=stringResult.."\n"
                for _ = 1,space do
                    stringResult=stringResult.."    "
                end
            end

            if type(Index) == "string" then
                stringResult=stringResult..'["'..tostring(Index)..'"]='
            elseif type(Index) == "number" then
                stringResult=stringResult..'['..tostring(Index)..']='
            elseif typeof(Index) == "Instance" then
                stringResult=stringResult..'['..tostring(Index:GetFullName())..']='
            end
            if type(Value) =="table" then
                stringResult=stringResult..tabletostring(Value,mode,space+1)
            else
                if typeof(Value) == "Instance" then
                    stringResult=stringResult..tostring(Value:GetFullName())
                elseif typeof(Value) == "string" then
                    stringResult=stringResult.."[["..tostring(Value).."]]"
                    else
                    stringResult=stringResult..tostring(Value)
                end
            end
            if amount ~= tablesize then
                stringResult=stringResult..","
            elseif mode == 2 then
                stringResult=stringResult.."\n"
            end
        end


    end
    for _ = 1,space do     stringResult=stringResult.."    "    end
    stringResult=stringResult.."}"

    return stringResult
end

function ElectionDataService:Start()

end;

function ElectionDataService:Init()
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
end;


return ElectionDataService

-- // Functions

local function basicTween(instance, properties, duration)
	local tween = TweenService:Create(
		instance,
		TweenInfo.new(
			duration,
			Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,
			Enum.EasingDirection.In,
			0,
			false,
			0
		),
		properties
	)

	tween:Play()

	if tween.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing or tween.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Begin then
		tween.Completed:Wait()
	end
end

local function createMushroomCloud(position, container, clouds, shockwave)
	local baseCloud = basePart:Clone()
	baseCloud.Position = position

	local poleBase = basePart:Clone()
	poleBase.Position = position + Vector3.new(0, 0.1, 0)

	local cloud1 = basePart:Clone()
	cloud1.Position = position + Vector3.new(0, 0.75, 0)

	local cloud2 = basePart:Clone()
	cloud2.Position = position + Vector3.new(0, 1.25, 0)

	local cloud3 = basePart:Clone()
	cloud3.Position = position + Vector3.new(0, 1.7, 0)

	local poleRing = basePart:Clone()
	poleRing.Position = position+Vector3.new(0, 1.3, 0)
	poleRing.Transparency = 0.2
	poleRing.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Dark stone grey")
	poleRing.CFrame = poleRing.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0)

	local mushCloud = basePart:Clone()
	mushCloud.Position = position+Vector3.new(0, 2.3, 0)

	local topCloud = basePart:Clone()
	topCloud.Position = position+Vector3.new(0, 2.7, 0)

	do
		local baseCloudMesh = cloudMesh:Clone()
		baseCloudMesh.Parent = baseCloud 
		baseCloudMesh.Scale = Vector3.new(2.5, 1, 4.5)

		local poleBaseMesh = cloudMesh:Clone()
		poleBaseMesh.Scale = Vector3.new(1.25, 2, 2.5)
		poleBaseMesh.Parent = poleBase

		local cloud1Mesh = cloudMesh:Clone()
		cloud1Mesh.Scale = Vector3.new(0.5, 3, 1)
		cloud1Mesh.Parent = cloud1

		local cloud2Mesh = cloudMesh:Clone()
		cloud2Mesh.Scale = Vector3.new(0.5, 1.5, 1)
		cloud2Mesh.Parent = cloud2

		local cloud3Mesh = cloudMesh:Clone()
		cloud3Mesh.Scale = Vector3.new(0.5, 1.5, 1)
		cloud3Mesh.Parent = cloud3

		local poleRingMesh = ringMesh:Clone()
		poleRingMesh.Scale = Vector3.new(1.2, 1.2, 1.2)
		poleRingMesh.Parent = poleRing

		local topCloudMesh = cloudMesh:Clone()
		topCloudMesh.Scale = Vector3.new(7.5, 1.5, 1.5)
		topCloudMesh.Parent = topCloud

		local mushCloudMesh = cloudMesh:Clone()
		mushCloudMesh.Scale = Vector3.new(2.5, 1.75, 3.5)
		mushCloudMesh.Parent = mushCloud
	end

	table.insert(clouds, baseCloud)
	table.insert(clouds, topCloud)
	table.insert(clouds, mushCloud)
	table.insert(clouds, cloud1)
	table.insert(clouds, cloud2)
	table.insert(clouds, cloud3)
	table.insert(clouds, poleBase)
	table.insert(clouds, poleRing)

	local bigRing = basePart:Clone()
	bigRing.Position = position
	bigRing.CFrame = bigRing.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0)

	local smallRing = basePart:Clone()
	smallRing.Position = position
	smallRing.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Dark stone grey")
	smallRing.CFrame = smallRing.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0)

	local innerSphere = basePart:Clone()
	innerSphere.Position = position
	innerSphere.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Bright orange")
	innerSphere.Transparency = 0.5

	local outterSphere = basePart:Clone()
	outterSphere.Position = position
	outterSphere.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Bright orange")
	outterSphere.Transparency = 0.5

	do
		local bigMesh = ringMesh:Clone()
		bigMesh.Scale = Vector3.new(5, 5, 1)
		bigMesh.Parent = bigRing

		local smallMesh = ringMesh:Clone()
		smallMesh.Scale = Vector3.new(4.6, 4.6, 1.5)
		smallMesh.Parent = smallRing

		local innerSphereMesh = sphereMesh:Clone()	
		innerSphereMesh.Scale = Vector3.new(-6.5, -6.5, -6.5)
		innerSphereMesh.Parent = innerSphere
	
		local outterSphereMesh = sphereMesh:Clone()
		outterSphereMesh.Scale = Vector3.new(6.5, 6.5, 6.5)
		outterSphereMesh.Parent = outterSphere
	end

	table.insert(shockwave, bigRing)	
	table.insert(shockwave, smallRing)
	table.insert(shockwave, outterSphere)
	table.insert(shockwave, innerSphere)

	for _, v in ipairs(shockwave) do
		v.Parent = container
	end
	for _, v in ipairs(clouds) do
		v.Parent = container
	end

	return {
		OutterSphere = outterSphere,
		InnerSphere = innerSphere,
		BigRing = bigRing,
		SmallRing = smallRing,
		BaseCloud = baseCloud,
		PoleBase = poleBase,
		PoleRing = poleRing,
		Cloud1 = cloud1,
		Cloud2 = cloud2,
		Cloud3 = cloud3,
		MushCloud = mushCloud,
		TopCloud = topCloud
	}
end

local function effects(nolighting)
	for i = 1, 2 do
		local explosionSound = Instance.new("Sound")
		explosionSound.Name = "NUKE_SOUND"
		explosionSound.SoundId = "http://www.roblox.com/asset?id=130768997"
		explosionSound.Volume = 0.5
		explosionSound.PlaybackSpeed = i / 2
		explosionSound.RollOffMinDistance, explosionSound.RollOffMaxDistance = 0, 10000
		explosionSound.Archivable = false
		explosionSound.Parent = SoundService
		explosionSound:Play()
		Debris:AddItem(explosionSound, 30)
	end

	if not nolighting then
		local oldBrightness = Lighting.Brightness
		Lighting.Brightness = 5

		basicTween(Lighting, {Brightness = 1}, 4 / 0.01 * (1 / 60))
		Lighting.Brightness = oldBrightness
	end
end

local function tagHumanoid(humanoid, attacker)
	local creatorTag = Instance.new("ObjectValue")
	creatorTag.Name = "creator"
	creatorTag.Value = attacker
	Debris:AddItem(creatorTag, 2)
	creatorTag.Parent = humanoid
end

local function destruction(position, radius, attacker)
	for _, v in ipairs(workspace:GetPartBoundsInRadius(position, radius, explosionParams)) do
		if v.ClassName ~= "Terrain" and v.Anchored == false then
			if attacker then
				local humanoid = v.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

				if humanoid and not humanoid:FindFirstChild("creator") then
					tagHumanoid(humanoid, attacker)
				end
			end

			v:BreakJoints()
			v.Material = Enum.Material.CorrodedMetal
			v.AssemblyLinearVelocity = CFrame.new(v.Position, position):VectorToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(math.random(-5, 5), 5, 1000))
		end
	end
end

local function explode(position: Vector3, explosionSize: number, nolighting: boolean?, attacker: (Player | Humanoid)?)
	-- // Setup
	local shockwaveCompleted = false
	explosionParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = nukeIgnore
	local clouds, shockwave = {}, {}
	local container = Instance.new("Model")
	container.Name = "ADONIS_NUCLEAREXPLOSION"
	container.Archivable = false
	container.Parent = workspace
	table.insert(nukeIgnore, container)

	-- // Create mushroom cloud
	local cloudData = createMushroomCloud(position, container, clouds, shockwave)
	local outterSphere, innerSphere, bigRing, smallRing = cloudData.OutterSphere, cloudData.InnerSphere, cloudData.BigRing, cloudData.SmallRing
	local baseCloud, poleBase, poleRing = cloudData.BaseCloud, cloudData.PoleBase, cloudData.PoleRing
	local cloud1, cloud2, cloud3, mushCloud, topCloud = cloudData.Cloud1, cloudData.Cloud2, cloudData.Cloud3, cloudData.MushCloud, cloudData.TopCloud

	-- // Lighting & audio effects
	local newSky = skybox:Clone()
	table.insert(nukeSkyboxes, newSky)
	newSky.Parent = Lighting
	task.spawn(effects, nolighting)

	for _, v in ipairs(Lighting:GetChildren()) do
		if v:IsA("Sky") and not table.find(nukeSkyboxes, v) and not table.find(realSkyboxes, v) then
			table.insert(realSkyboxes, v)
		end
	end

	-- // Shockwave
	task.spawn(function()
		local maxSize = explosionSize * 3
		local smallSize = explosionSize / 2.5
		local nukeDuration = (maxSize - smallSize) / 2 * (1 / 60)
		local transforms = {
			{innerSphere, Vector3.new(-6.5 * maxSize, -6.5 * maxSize, -6.5 * maxSize)},
			{outterSphere, Vector3.new(6.5 * maxSize, 6.5 * maxSize, 6.5 * maxSize)},
			{smallRing, Vector3.new(4.6 * maxSize, 4.6 * maxSize, 1.5 * maxSize)},
			{bigRing, Vector3.new(5 * maxSize,5 * maxSize,1 * maxSize)},
		}

		for _, v in ipairs(transforms) do
			local object, scale = v[1], v[2]

			if typeof(object) == "Instance" then
				local mesh = object:FindFirstChildOfClass("SpecialMesh")

				if mesh then
					mesh.Scale = scale * (smallSize / maxSize)

					task.spawn(basicTween, mesh, {Scale = scale}, nukeDuration)
				end
			end
		end

		do
			local startclock = os.clock()
			local expGrow, expStat = maxSize - smallSize, smallSize

			repeat
				destruction(
					position,
					(((os.clock() - startclock) / nukeDuration) * expGrow + expStat) * 2,
					attacker
				)
				task.wait(1/25)
			until (os.clock() - startclock) > nukeDuration
		end

		for _, v in ipairs(shockwave) do
			v.Transparency = 0

			task.spawn(
				basicTween,
				v,
				{Transparency = 1},
				100 * (1 / 60)
			)
		end
		task.wait(100 * (1 / 60))

		for _ ,v in ipairs(shockwave) do
			v:Destroy()
		end

		shockwaveCompleted = true
	end)

	-- // Mushroom cloud grow
	task.spawn(function()
		local transforms = {
			{baseCloud, Vector3.new(2.5 * explosionSize, 1 * explosionSize, 4.5 * explosionSize), Vector3.new(0, 0.05 * explosionSize, 0)},
			{poleBase, Vector3.new(1 * explosionSize, 2 * explosionSize, 2.5 * explosionSize), Vector3.new(0, 0.1 * explosionSize, 0)},
			{poleRing, Vector3.new(1.2 * explosionSize, 1.2 * explosionSize, 1.2 * explosionSize), Vector3.new(0, 1.3 * explosionSize, 0)},
			{topCloud, Vector3.new(0.75 * explosionSize, 1.5 * explosionSize, 1.5 * explosionSize), Vector3.new(0, 2.7 * explosionSize, 0)},
			{mushCloud, Vector3.new(2.5 * explosionSize, 1.75 * explosionSize, 3.5 * explosionSize), Vector3.new(0, 2.3 * explosionSize, 0)},
			{cloud1, Vector3.new(0.5 * explosionSize, 3 * explosionSize, 1*  explosionSize), Vector3.new(0, 0.75 * explosionSize, 0)},
			{cloud2, Vector3.new(0.5 * explosionSize, 1.5 * explosionSize, 1 * explosionSize), Vector3.new(0, 1.25 * explosionSize, 0)},
			{cloud3, Vector3.new(0.5 * explosionSize, 1.5 * explosionSize, 1 * explosionSize), Vector3.new(0, 1.7 * explosionSize, 0)},
		}

		for _, v in ipairs(transforms) do
			local object, scale = v[1], v[2]

			if typeof(object) == "Instance" then
				object.Position = position + v[3] / 5
				local mesh = object:FindFirstChildOfClass("SpecialMesh")

				if mesh then
					mesh.Scale = scale / 5

					task.spawn(basicTween, mesh, {Scale = scale}, 2)
				end

				task.spawn(basicTween, object, {Position = position + v[3]}, 2)
			end
		end
	end)
	task.wait(2)

	-- // Mushroom cloud de-heating to red
	for _, v in ipairs(clouds) do
		local mesh = v:FindFirstChildOfClass("SpecialMesh")

		if mesh then
			mesh.VertexColor = Vector3.new(0.9, 0.6, 0)
			task.spawn(
				basicTween,
				mesh,
				{VertexColor = Vector3.new(0.9, 0, 0)},
				0.6 / 0.0025 * (1 / 60)
			)
		end
	end
	task.wait(0.6 / 0.0025 * (1 / 60))

	-- // Mushroom cloud de-heating to black
	for _, v in ipairs(clouds) do
		local mesh = v:FindFirstChildOfClass("SpecialMesh")

		if mesh then
			mesh.VertexColor = Vector3.new(0.9, 0, 0)
			task.spawn(
				basicTween,
				mesh,
				{VertexColor = Vector3.new(0.5, 0, 0)},
				(0.9 - 0.5) / 0.01 * (1 / 60) * 2
			)
		end
	end
	task.wait((0.9 - 0.5) / 0.01 * (1 / 60) * 2)

	local skyConnection
	skyConnection = newSky.AncestryChanged:Connect(function()
		if newSky and newSky.Parent ~= Lighting and table.find(nukeSkyboxes, newSky) then
			table.remove(nukeSkyboxes, table.find(nukeSkyboxes, newSky))
		end

		local hasNukeSkyboxes = false

		for _, v in ipairs(nukeSkyboxes) do
			if v.Parent == Lighting then
				hasNukeSkyboxes = true
				break
			end
		end

		if not hasNukeSkyboxes then
			for i = #realSkyboxes, 1, -1 do
				local v = realSkyboxes[i]

				if v.Parent == Lighting then
					v.Parent = nil

					task.spawn(function()
						task.wait()
						v.Parent = Lighting
					end)
				elseif table.find(realSkyboxes, v) then
					table.remove(realSkyboxes, table.find(realSkyboxes, v))
				end
			end
		end

		skyConnection:Disconnect()
	end)
	Debris:AddItem(newSky, 10)

	-- // De-heated cloud becoming natural cloud like (no longer heat or nuclear)
	for _, v in ipairs(clouds) do
		local mesh = v:FindFirstChildOfClass("SpecialMesh")

		if mesh then
			mesh.VertexColor = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
			task.spawn(
				basicTween,
				mesh,
				{VertexColor = Vector3.new(0.5, 0.5, 0.5)},
				0.5 / 0.005 * (1 / 60)
			)
			task.spawn(
				basicTween,
				mesh,
				{Scale = mesh.Scale + Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1) * (0.5 / 0.005)},
				0.5 / 0.005 * (1 / 60)
			)
		end

		task.spawn(
			basicTween,
			v,
			{Transparency = 0.5},
			0.5 / 0.005 * (1 / 60)
		)
	end
	task.wait(0.5 / 0.005 * (1 / 60))

	-- // Cloud dissapate
	for _, v in ipairs(clouds) do
		task.spawn(
			basicTween,
			v,
			{Transparency = 1},
			20
		)

		local mesh = v:FindFirstChildOfClass("SpecialMesh")

		if mesh then
			task.spawn(
				basicTween,
				mesh,
				{Scale = mesh.Scale + Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1) * (1 / 0.005)},
				20
			)
		end
	end
	task.wait(20)

	while true do task.wait(1) if shockwaveCompleted then break end end
	container:Destroy()
end


return explode

--[[
    Filter (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53

local Filter = {};

local textService = game:GetService('TextService');

local pcall = pcall;
local filterStringAsync = textService.FilterStringAsync;

function Filter.FilterStringAsync(string, fromUserID, textContext)
    local suc, filterResult = pcall(filterStringAsync, textService, string, fromUserID, textContext);
    if not suc then return; end;
    return filterResult;
end;

function Filter.GetChatForUserAsync(filterResult, toUserID)
    local suc, filtered = pcall(filterResult.GetChatForUserAsync, filterResult, toUserID);
    if not suc then return; end;
    return filtered;
end;

return Filter;

--[[
    Fire (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Fire
-- Khizzer
-- February 23, 2023



local Trove;

local Fire = {}
Fire.__index = Fire

local SmokePrefab: ParticleEmitter;
local Signal;


function Fire.new(collectionServiceInstance: Instance)

	local self = setmetatable({}, Fire)

	self.Trove = Trove.new();
	self.CollectionServiceInstance = collectionServiceInstance;

	local effectContainer = Instance.new('Folder');
	effectContainer.Parent = collectionServiceInstance;

	self.EffectContainer = effectContainer;
	self.FireEndedSignal = Signal.new();

	self.Trove:Add(effectContainer);
	self.Trove:Add(effectContainer.DescendantRemoving:Connect(function(descendant)
		if not effectContainer:FindFirstChildWhichIsA('BasePart') then
			self.FireEndedSignal:Fire();
			self.Trove:Clean();
		end;
	end));

	task.defer(function()
		task.wait(1200)
		if effectContainer:FindFirstChildWhichIsA('BasePart') then
			self.FireEndedSignal:Fire();
			self.Trove:Clean();
		end
	end)

	collectionServiceInstance:SetAttribute('Running', true);

	return self
end;

function Fire:BurnPart(part: BasePart, smoke: boolean?)
	part.Parent = self.EffectContainer;

	local attachment = Instance.new('Attachment');
	attachment.Parent = part;

	if smoke then
		local smokeEmitter = SmokePrefab:Clone();
		smokeEmitter.Parent = attachment;
	end;

	local fireEmitter = Instance.new('Fire')
	fireEmitter.Parent = attachment;
	fireEmitter.Size = 15;
	fireEmitter:SetAttribute('Health', 100);
end;

function Fire:Init()
	Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
	SmokePrefab = self.ServerAssets.SmokePrefab;
	Signal = self.Shared.Signal;
end;


return Fire

--[[
    Functions (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Functions
-- Khizzer
-- July 12, 2021



local Functions = {}

function Functions:Create(obj)
	obj = Instance.new(obj)
	return function (props)
		for prop, val in next, props do
			obj[prop] = val
		end
		return obj
	end
end 

function Functions:GetMass(part)
    local density = PhysicalProperties.new(part.Material).Density
	local size    = part.Size
	local volume  = size.x * size.y * size.x
	return density * volume
end



return Functions


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Modules/GlobalStorage.lua ---

--[[
    GlobalStorage (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
--[[

	GlobalStorage
	by boatbomber (c) 2021

	This is a module for handling data that can be read from/written to
	from multiple servers at a time. It is made only for commutative updates.
	This is so that your operations can be applied locally and globally at different
	times and still end up at the same value eventually. Uses MemoryStore for atomic locking.

	Make sure your transform function is deterministic and has no side effects,
	as it will be run twice- once locally and once globally. If it absolutely must,
	then it can take in a second arguement, a boolean "isGlobal" that is true when being
	run globally and false during the local run.

	Examples:

		local PlayerStore = GlobalStorage.new("User_1234", 1234)
		local DEFAULT_COINS = 100
		-- Can be used to safely +/- number stores
		local coins = PlayerStore:Get("Coins", DEFAULT_COINS)
		PlayerStore:Update("Coins", function(oldValue)
			return (oldValue or DEFAULT_COINS) + 5
		end)
		coins = PlayerStore:Get("Coins", DEFAULT_COINS)
		-- Can be used to safely add/remove unique dict keys
		local notifications = PlayerStore:Get("Notifications", {})
		PlayerStore:Update("Notifications", function(oldValue)
			return (oldValue or {})[GUID] = newNotif
		end)
		notifications = PlayerStore:Get("Notifications", {})
--]]

local DEBUG = false
local function dprint(...)
	if DEBUG then
		print(...)
	end
end

local DataStoreService = game:GetService("DataStoreService")
local MemoryStoreService = game:GetService("MemoryStoreService")
local MessagingService = game:GetService("MessagingService")

local GlobalStorage = {
	_cache = {},
}

function GlobalStorage.new(name: string, associatedUserId: number?)
	local debugInfo = string.format("GlobalStorage '%s'", name)

	-- Get existing store object if possible
	if GlobalStorage._cache[name] then
		dprint(debugInfo, "got existing store")
		local cachedStore = GlobalStorage._cache[name]
		cachedStore._references += 1
		return cachedStore
	end

	-- Create new store object
	dprint(debugInfo, "created new store")
	local Store = {
		_dsStore = DataStoreService:GetDataStore(name),
		_msMap = MemoryStoreService:GetSortedMap(name),
		_associatedUserId = associatedUserId,
		_references = 1,
		_cache = {},
		_msgId = "BS_" .. name,
		_updateQueue = {},
		_events = {},
		_destroyed = false,
		_flushesInProgress = {},
	}

	function Store:_flushUpdateQueue()
		if next(self._updateQueue) == nil then
			dprint(debugInfo, "update queue empty, cancelling flush")
			return
		end

		dprint(debugInfo, "flushing update queue")
		for key, transformers in pairs(self._updateQueue) do
			if self._flushesInProgress[key] then
				dprint(debugInfo, "flush already in progress for key", key)
				continue
			end
			if #transformers < 1 then
				dprint(debugInfo, "no transformers for key", key)
				self._updateQueue[key] = nil
				continue
			end
			self._flushesInProgress[key] = true

			-- DataStore UpdateAsync can conflict with other servers if called at the exact same time
			-- and race so whichever finishes last will overwrite the previous.
			-- MemoryStore UpdateAsync solves this by retrying if two are called at once, so we use
			-- that as a locking mechanism to avoid two DataStore updates overwriting. If two try to grab
			-- while unlocked, MemoryStore will force one of them to retry later.

			local unlocked, lockWaitTime = false, 0
			while unlocked == false do
				local success, message = pcall(function()
					dprint(debugInfo, "attempting to retrieve lock for", key)
					self._msMap:UpdateAsync(key, function(lockOwner)
						if lockOwner ~= nil then
							dprint("Lock already taken by " .. lockOwner)
							return nil -- Someone else has this key rn, we must wait
						end

						unlocked = true

						-- Since other servers trying to take it will be returning
						-- different JobId, memorystore will know its a conflict
						-- and force the others to retry
						return game.JobId
					end, 15)
				end)
				if not success then
					warn(message)
				end

				if unlocked == false then
					lockWaitTime += task.wait()
					if lockWaitTime > 60 then
						warn(
							"Update flush for "
								.. key
								.. " expired after 60 seconds while waiting for lock to be available."
						)
						self._flushesInProgress[key] = nil
						return
					end
					dprint(debugInfo, "waiting for lock for", key, "for", lockWaitTime, "seconds so far")
				end
			end
			dprint(debugInfo, "received lock for", key)

			-- Update the global value
			dprint(debugInfo, "updating global value for", key)
			self._dsStore:UpdateAsync(key, function(storedValue)
				local value = storedValue

				for i, transformer in ipairs(transformers) do
					local success, newValue = pcall(transformer, value, true)
					if not success then
						warn(newValue)
						dprint(debugInfo, "cancelled transformer", i, "on", key)
						continue -- skip this one, transform errored
					end

					if newValue == nil then
						dprint(debugInfo, "skipped transformer", i, "on", key)
						continue -- skip this one, transform exited
					end

					dprint(debugInfo, "applied transformer", i, "on", key)
					value = newValue
				end
				table.clear(transformers)

				self._cache[key] = value

				-- Inform other servers they need to refresh
				task.defer(function()
					local publishSuccess, publishResult = pcall(function()
						dprint(debugInfo, "informing other servers of changes to", key)
						MessagingService:PublishAsync(self._msgId, {
							JobId = game.JobId,
							Key = key,
						})
					end)
					if not publishSuccess then
						warn(publishResult)
					end
				end)

				return value
			end)

			-- Unlock this key for the next server to take
			dprint(debugInfo, "unlocking", key)
			self._flushesInProgress[key] = nil
			pcall(self._msMap.RemoveAsync, self._msMap, key)
		end
	end

	function Store:GetKeyChangedSignal(key: string)
		local event = self._events[key]
		if not event then
			event = Instance.new("BindableEvent")
			self._events[key] = event
		end
		return event.Event
	end

	function Store:Get(key: string, default: any?, skipCache: boolean?)
		if not skipCache and self._cache[key] ~= nil then
			dprint(debugInfo, "getting local value of", key)
			return self._cache[key] or default
		end

		dprint(debugInfo, "getting global value of", key)

		local value = self._dsStore:GetAsync(key)

		if value == nil then
			value = default
		end

		self._cache[key] = value
		return value
	end

	function Store:Update(key: string, transformer: (any?, boolean?) -> any?)
		-- Queue it up for updating on the latest real value & replication
		dprint(debugInfo, "queuing global transformer for", key)
		if self._updateQueue[key] == nil then
			self._updateQueue[key] = { transformer }
		else
			table.insert(self._updateQueue[key], transformer)
		end

		-- First, perform it locally
		dprint(debugInfo, "applying local transformer for", key)
		local success, newValue = pcall(transformer, self._cache[key], false)
		if not success then
			warn(newValue)
			return -- cancel, transform errored
		end

		if newValue == nil then
			return -- cancel, transform exited
		end

		self._cache[key] = newValue
		local event = self._events[key]
		if event then
			event:Fire(newValue)
		end
	end

	function Store:Destroy()
		if self._destroyed then
			dprint(debugInfo, "is already destroyed")
			return
		end

		self._references -= 1
		if self._references > 0 then
			dprint(debugInfo, "removing a reference to the store, there are now", self._references, "references")
			return
		end

		dprint(debugInfo, "destroying store!")
		self._destroyed = true

		if self._msgConnection ~= nil then
			self._msgConnection:Disconnect()
		end

		for _, event in pairs(self._events) do
			event:Destroy()
		end

		GlobalStorage._cache[name] = nil

		self:_flushUpdateQueue()

		while next(self._flushesInProgress) do
			dprint(debugInfo, "Waiting for flushes to finish before wiping")
			task.wait()
		end

		table.clear(self)
		self._destroyed = true
	end

	task.spawn(function()
		-- Subscribe to store's msg for cross-server updates
		local subscribeSuccess, subscribeConnection = pcall(function()
			return MessagingService:SubscribeAsync(Store._msgId, function(message)
				if game.JobId == message.Data.JobId then
					return
				end

				if (Store._destroyed) or (Store._cache == nil) then
					error(debugInfo .. " received update from another server after being destroyed")
					return
				end

				local key = message.Data.Key
				dprint(debugInfo, "received update to", key, "from another server")

				local newValue = Store:Get(key, Store._cache[key], true)
				local event = Store._events[key]
				if event then
					event:Fire(newValue)
				end
			end)
		end)
		if subscribeSuccess then
			if Store._destroyed then
				dprint(debugInfo, "destroyed during subscribe, disconnecting subscription")
				subscribeConnection:Disconnect()
			else
				Store._msgConnection = subscribeConnection
			end
		else
			warn(subscribeConnection)
		end

		-- Start update queue flush thread
		while not Store._destroyed do
			local jitter = math.random(0, 100) / 100 -- Reduce server conflicts?
			task.wait(6 + jitter)
			-- Check if destroyed during wait
			if Store._destroyed then break end

			dprint(debugInfo, "periodically flushing update queue")
			Store:_flushUpdateQueue()
		end
	end)

	-- Cache the store object for future GetStore sharing
	GlobalStorage._cache[name] = Store
	return Store
end

game:BindToClose(function()
	for _, Store in pairs(GlobalStorage._cache) do
		task.spawn(Store._flushUpdateQueue, Store)
	end
end)

game.Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(Player)
	for name, Store in pairs(GlobalStorage._cache) do
		if Store._associatedUserId == Player.UserId then
			dprint(string.format("Destroying %s store for %s on leave", name, Player.Name))
			Store:Destroy()
		end
	end
end)

return GlobalStorage
